5. The emission limit values cannot in any case be achieved through dilution with waters taken exclusively for this purpose. It is in any case not permitted to dilute with cooling, washing, or waters taken exclusively for the purpose the partial discharges of paragraph 4, before their treatment to adapt them to the limits provided for by the third part of this decree. The competent authority, in the authorization phase, may prescribe that the discharge of cooling, washing waters, or waters used for the production of energy be separated from the terminal discharge of each establishment.
6. If the waters taken from a surface water body present parameters with values higher than the emission limit values, the discipline of the discharge is established on the basis of the nature of the alterations and the quality objectives of the receiving water body. In any case, the waters must be returned with qualitative characteristics not worse than those taken and without increases in flow rate to the same water body from which they were taken.
7. Without prejudice to what is provided for in Article 112, for the purposes of the discipline of discharges and authorizations, the following wastewater is assimilated to domestic wastewater:
a) from companies dedicated exclusively to the cultivation of the land and/or forestry;
b) from companies dedicated to livestock breeding that, as regards livestock effluents, practice agronomic use in conformity with the regional discipline established on the basis of the criteria and general technical norms of Article 112, paragraph 2, and that have at least one hectare of agricultural land for each of the quantities indicated in Table 6 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree;
c) from companies dedicated to the activities of letters a) and b) that also exercise transformation or enhancement activities of agricultural production, inserted with a character of normality and functional complementarity in the company's production cycle and with raw material coming mainly from the cultivation activity of the land of which one has availability for any reason;
d) from aquaculture and fish farming plants that give rise to a discharge and that are characterized by a breeding density equal to or less than 1 kg per square meter of water surface or in which a water flow rate equal to or less than 50 liters per minute second is used;
e) having qualitative characteristics equivalent to domestic ones and indicated by the regional regulations;
f) from thermal activities, without prejudice to the regional sector disciplines.
8. Within six months from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, and subsequently every two years, the regions transmit to the Minister of the Environment and the Protection of the Territory and the Sea, to the Geological Survey of Italy - Soil Protection Department of the Agency for Environmental Protection and for Technical Services (APAT), and to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) the information relating to the functionality of the purifiers, as well as to the disposal of the relative sludge, according to the methods of Article 75, paragraph 5.
9. In order to ensure the widest dissemination of information on the state of the environment, the regions publish every two years, on their Official Bulletins and institutional internet sites, a report on the urban wastewater disposal activities in their areas of competence, according to the methods indicated in the decree of Article 75, paragraph 5.
10. The competent Authorities may promote and stipulate program agreements and contracts with interested economic subjects, in order to favor water saving, the reuse of discharge waters, and the recovery as raw material of the purification sludge, with the possibility of resorting to economic instruments, of establishing simplifications in administrative fulfilments and of setting, for the substances considered useful, limits on discharges in derogation of the general discipline, in any case respecting the community norms and the necessary measures for the achievement of the quality objectives.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 102**
**Discharges of thermal waters**
1. For thermal waters that present at the origin chemical parameters with values higher than the emission limit values, a derogation from the same values is permitted provided that the waters are returned with qualitative characteristics not higher than those taken or that the same, within the maximum of 10 percent, respect the bacteriological parameters and the hazardous substances of Tables 3/A and 5 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree are not present.
2. Thermal discharges are permitted, without prejudice to the discipline of the authorizations adopted by the regions pursuant to Article 124, paragraph 5:
a) in surface water bodies, provided that their discharge into the receiving body does not compromise the uses of the water resources and does not cause damage to health and the environment;
b) on the soil or in the surface layers of the subsoil, after verification of the geological situations;
c) in sewerage networks, provided that the regulations issued by the manager of the integrated water service are observed and they are authorized by the Area Authorities;
d) in separate sewerage networks provided for meteoric waters.

**Art. 103**
**Discharges on the soil**
1. It is forbidden to discharge on the soil or in the surface layers of the subsoil, with the exception of:
a) for the cases provided for by Article 100, paragraph 3;
b) for the overflow spillways serving the sewerage networks;
c) for the discharges of urban and industrial wastewater for which the technical impossibility or excessive costliness, in the face of the achievable environmental benefits, to discharge into surface water bodies is ascertained, provided that the same comply with the criteria and emission limit values set for this purpose by the regions pursuant to Article 101, paragraph 2. Until the issuance of new regional norms, the emission limit values of Table 4 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree apply;
d) for the discharges of waters from the processing of natural rocks as well as from the plants for washing mineral substances, provided that the relative sludge consists exclusively of water and natural inerts and does not cause damage to the aquifers or instability of the soils;
e) for the discharges of meteoric waters conveyed in separate sewerage networks;
f) for the waters deriving from the overflow of water reservoirs, from the maintenance operations of the water supply networks, and from the maintenance of the aqueduct wells.
2. Outside the hypotheses provided for in paragraph 1, the existing discharges on the soil must be conveyed into surface water bodies, in sewerage networks, or destined for reuse in conformity with the prescriptions set with the decree of Article 99, paragraph 1. In case of non-fulfillment of the indicated obligations, the authorization for discharge is considered for all effects revoked.
3. The discharges of letter c) of paragraph 1 must comply with the limits of Table 4 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree. The prohibition of discharge on the soil of the substances indicated at point 2.1 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree remains firm in any case.

**Art. 104**
**Discharges into the subsoil and groundwater**
1. Direct discharge into groundwater and the subsoil is prohibited.
2. By way of derogation from the provisions of paragraph 1, the competent authority, after a preliminary investigation, may authorize discharges into the same aquifer of water used for geothermal purposes, infiltration water from mines or quarries, or water pumped during specific civil engineering works, including those from heat exchange systems.
3. By way of derogation from the provisions of paragraph 1, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in agreement with the Minister of Productive Activities for offshore deposits and also with the regions for onshore deposits, may also authorize the discharge of water resulting from the extraction of hydrocarbons into the deep geological units from which the hydrocarbons themselves were extracted, or into units with the same characteristics, which contain or have contained hydrocarbons, indicating the discharge methods. The discharge must not contain other wastewater or other hazardous substances, different in quality and quantity, from those derived from the separation of hydrocarbons. The relevant authorizations are issued with the prescription of the necessary technical precautions to ensure that the discharged water cannot reach other water systems or harm other ecosystems.
4. By way of derogation from the provisions of paragraph 1, the competent authority, after a preliminary investigation also aimed at verifying the absence of foreign substances, may authorize discharges into the same aquifer of water used for the washing and processing of inert materials, provided that the relative sludge consists exclusively of water and natural inert materials and their discharge does not cause damage to the aquifer. To this end, the regionally competent Regional Agency for Environmental Protection (ARPA), at the expense of the subject requesting the authorization, shall ascertain the quantitative and qualitative characteristics of the sludge and the absence of possible damage to the aquifer, expressing a binding opinion on the request for discharge authorization.
5. For the activities of prospecting, exploration, and extraction of liquid or gaseous hydrocarbons at sea, the direct discharge of water into the sea shall occur according to the methods provided for by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea by his own decree, provided that the concentration of mineral oils is less than 40 mg/l. The direct discharge into the sea is progressively replaced by injection or reinjection into deep geological units, as soon as no longer productive wells suitable for injection or reinjection become available, and must in any case occur in compliance with the provisions of paragraphs 2 and 3.
6. The Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, when authorizing discharge into deep geological units as per paragraph 3, also authorizes direct discharge into the sea, according to the methods provided for in paragraphs 5 and 7, for the following cases:
a) for the fraction of excess water, if the capacity of the injector or reinjector well is not sufficient to guarantee the reception of all the water resulting from the extraction of hydrocarbons;
b) for the time necessary to carry out ordinary and extraordinary maintenance, aimed at guaranteeing the correct functionality and safety of the system consisting of the well and the injection or reinjection plant.
7. The direct discharge into the sea of the waters referred to in paragraphs 5 and 6 is authorized upon presentation of a monitoring plan aimed at verifying the absence of dangers for the water and for the aquatic ecosystems.
8. Apart from the cases provided for in paragraphs 2, 3, 5, and 7, existing and duly authorized discharges into the subsoil and groundwater must be conveyed into surface water bodies or destined, where possible, for recycling, reuse, or agronomic utilization. In case of non-compliance with the indicated obligations, the discharge authorization is revoked.

**Art. 105**
**Discharges into surface waters**
1. Discharges of industrial wastewater into surface waters must comply with the emission limit values set pursuant to Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2, as a function of the pursuit of quality objectives.
2. Discharges of urban wastewater that flow into sewerage networks, originating from agglomerations with fewer than 2,000 population equivalents and discharging into freshwaters and transitional waters, and discharges from agglomerations with fewer than 10,000 population equivalents, discharging into marine-coastal waters, are subject to appropriate treatment, in accordance with the indications of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree.
3. Urban wastewater must be subjected, before discharge, to secondary treatment or an equivalent treatment in accordance with the indications of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree.
4. The discharges provided for in paragraph 3 must also comply with the emission limit values set pursuant to Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2.
5. The regions shall issue specific regulations for the discharges from sewerage networks originating from agglomerations with high seasonal fluctuation of inhabitants, taking into account the provisions of paragraphs 2 and 3 and without prejudice to the achievement of quality objectives.
6. Discharges of urban wastewater into waters located in high mountain areas, i.e., above 1500 meters above sea level, where, due to low temperatures, it is difficult to carry out effective biological treatment, may be subjected to a less advanced treatment than that provided for in paragraph 3, provided that specific studies prove that the said discharges will not have negative repercussions on the environment.

**Art. 106**
**Discharges of urban wastewater into water bodies located in sensitive areas**
1. Without prejudice to the provisions of Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2, urban wastewater from agglomerations with more than 10,000 population equivalents, which discharges into receiving waters identified as sensitive areas, must be subjected to a more advanced treatment than that provided for in Article 105, paragraph 3, according to the specific requirements indicated in Annex 5 to the third part of this decree.
2. The provisions of paragraph 1 do not apply in sensitive areas where it can be demonstrated that the minimum percentage of reduction of the total load entering all urban wastewater treatment plants is at least seventy-five percent for total phosphorus or at least seventy-five percent for total nitrogen.
3. The regions shall identify, among the discharges from urban wastewater treatment plants located within the drainage basins afferent to sensitive areas, those which, by contributing to the pollution of such areas, are to be subjected to the treatment referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2 in function of achieving the quality objective of the receiving water bodies.

**Art. 107**
**Discharges into sewerage networks**
1. Without prejudice to the non-derogability of the emission limit values referred to in table 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree and, limited to the parameters referred to in note 2 of Table 5 of the same Annex 5, to Table 3, discharges of industrial wastewater that discharge into sewerage networks are subject to the technical standards, regulatory requirements, and limit values adopted by the competent Area Authority based on the characteristics of the plant, and in such a way as to ensure the protection of the receiving water body as well as compliance with the regulations for discharges of urban wastewater defined pursuant to Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2.
2. Discharges of domestic wastewater that discharge into sewerage networks are always permitted provided they comply with the regulations issued by the manager of the integrated water service and approved by the competent Area Authority.
3. The disposal of waste, even if shredded, into the sewer system is not permitted, with the exception of organic waste from food scraps, mixed with water from civil uses, treated through the installation, previously communicated to the manager of the integrated water service, of food waste disposers that reduce its mass into fine particles, after a technical check of the plants and networks by the manager of the integrated water service who is responsible for the proper functioning of the system.
4. The regions, having heard the provinces, may establish supplementary rules for the control of discharges from civil and productive settlements connected to public sewers, for the functionality of pretreatment plants, and for compliance with the limits and prescriptions provided for in the relevant authorizations.

**Art. 108**
**Discharges of hazardous substances**
1. The provisions relating to the discharge of hazardous substances apply to establishments in which activities are carried out that involve the production, transformation, or use of the substances referred to in Tables 3/A and 5 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, and in whose discharges the presence of such substances is ascertained in quantities or concentrations exceeding the limits of detectability permitted by the detection methods in force on the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, or, subsequently, exceeding the limits of detectability permitted by the updates to such methods developed pursuant to point 4 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree.
2. Taking into account the toxicity, persistence, and bioaccumulation of the substance considered in the environment where the discharge is made, the competent authority, when issuing the authorization, may set, in cases where it is ascertained that the limit values defined pursuant to Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2, prevent or prejudice the achievement of the quality objectives provided for in the protection plan referred to in Article 121, also due to the co-presence of other discharges of hazardous substances, emission limit values more restrictive than those set pursuant to Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2.
3. For the purposes of implementing the provisions of paragraph 1 of Article 107 and paragraph 2 of this article, the prescriptions concerning the discharges of companies subject to the provisions of Legislative Decree No. 59 of 18 February 2005 must be implemented by 30 October 2007. These prescriptions, concerning emission limit values, parameters, and technical measures, are based on the best available techniques, without the obligation to use a specific technique or technology, taking into account the technical characteristics of the plant in question, its geographical location, and the local environmental conditions.
4. For the substances referred to in Table 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, deriving from the production cycles indicated in the same table, the authorizations shall also establish the maximum quantity of the substance expressed in units of weight per unit of characteristic element of the polluting activity, that is, per raw material or per unit of product, in accordance with what is indicated in the same Table. Discharges containing the hazardous substances referred to in paragraph 1 are subject to the prescriptions of point 1.2.3. of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree.
5. For industrial wastewater containing the substances of Table 5 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, the discharge measurement point is fixed as provided for by the integrated environmental authorization of Legislative Decree No. 59 of 18 February 2005, and, in the case of activities not falling within the scope of the aforementioned decree, immediately after leaving the establishment or the treatment plant that serves the establishment itself. The competent authority may request that partial discharges containing the substances of table 5 of the same Annex 5 be kept separate from the general discharge and regulated as waste. If the industrial wastewater treatment plant that treats the hazardous substances, referred to in table 5 of the same Annex 5, receives wastewater containing hazardous substances not sensitive to the type of treatment adopted, the competent authority, during authorization, will appropriately reduce the emission limit values indicated in table 3 of the same Annex 5 for each of the aforesaid hazardous substances indicated in Table 5, taking into account the dilution caused by the mixing of the different wastewaters.
6. The authority competent to issue the authorization for the substances referred to in Table 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, deriving from the production cycles indicated in the same table, shall draw up a list of the authorizations issued, of the existing discharges, and of the checks carried out, for the purpose of their subsequent forwarding to the European Commission.

**CHAPTER IV - FURTHER MEASURES FOR THE PROTECTION OF WATER BODIES**

**Art. 109**
**Dumping at sea of material from dredging and from the laying of cables and pipelines**
1. For the purpose of protecting the marine environment and in accordance with the provisions of international conventions in force on the matter, the deliberate dumping into the sea from ships or aircraft and from structures located in the waters of the sea or in areas contiguous to it, such as beaches, lagoons and brackish ponds and coastal embankments, of the following materials is permitted:
a) materials from the dredging of marine or brackish seabeds or of emerged coastal lands;
b) inert materials, inorganic geological materials, and manufactured articles for the sole purpose of use, where their compatibility and environmental harmlessness are demonstrated;
c) organic and inorganic material of marine or brackish origin, produced during fishing activities carried out in the sea or lagoon or brackish ponds.
2. Authorization for the dumping at sea of the materials referred to in paragraph 1, letter a), is issued by the competent authority only when, within the relevant preliminary investigation, the technical or economic impossibility of their use for beach nourishment or recovery or of their alternative disposal in accordance with the methods established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Infrastructure and Transport, of Agricultural and Forestry Policies, of Productive Activities, after agreement with the permanent Conference for relations between the State, the regions and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, to be issued within one hundred and twenty days from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, is demonstrated.
3. The dumping at sea of material referred to in paragraph 1, letter b), is subject to authorization, with the exclusion of new manufactured articles subject to environmental impact assessment. For restoration works, which do not involve an increase in the volume of pre-existing works, only communication to the competent authority is required.
4. The dumping at sea of the materials referred to in paragraph 1, letter c), is not subject to authorization.
5. The movement of the seabed resulting from the activity of laying cables and pipelines at sea is subject to regional authorization issued in accordance with the technical methods established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Productive Activities, of Infrastructure and Transport and of Agricultural and Forestry Policies, for their respective competencies, to be issued within one hundred and twenty days from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree. In the case of pipelines or cables that are part of energy networks of national interest, or for connection with energy networks of other states, the authorization is issued by the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, after consulting the interested regions, within the single authorization procedure for the networks themselves.

**Art. 110**
**Treatment of waste at urban wastewater treatment plants**
1. Except as provided in paragraphs 2 and 3, the use of urban wastewater treatment plants for the disposal of waste is prohibited.
2. By way of derogation from paragraph 1, the competent authority, in agreement with the Area Authority, in relation to particular needs and within the limits of the residual treatment capacity, may authorize the manager of the integrated water service to dispose of liquid waste in the urban wastewater treatment plant, limited to types compatible with the purification process.
3. The manager of the integrated water service, upon communication to the competent authority pursuant to Article 124, is in any case authorized to accept in plants with adequate characteristics and purification capacity, which respect the limit values referred to in Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2, the following waste and materials, provided they originate from its own optimal territorial area or from another optimal territorial area lacking adequate plants:
a) waste consisting of wastewater that respects the limit values established for discharge into the sewer system;
b) waste consisting of material from the ordinary maintenance of domestic wastewater treatment systems provided for under Article 100, paragraph 3;
c) materials deriving from the ordinary maintenance of the sewerage network as well as those deriving from other urban wastewater treatment plants, in which the further treatment of the same is not technically and/or economically feasible.
4. The activity referred to in paragraphs 2 and 3 may be permitted provided that the possible reuse of the wastewater and sludge is not compromised.
5. In the communication provided for in paragraph 3, the manager of the integrated water service must indicate the residual capacity of the plant and the characteristics and quantities of the waste he intends to treat. The competent authority may indicate different quantities or prohibit the treatment of specific categories of waste. The competent authority shall also provide for the registration in special lists of the managers of treatment plants who have made the communication referred to in paragraph 3.
6. For the disposal of the waste referred to in paragraphs 2 and 3, the specific tariff determined by the Area Authority applies.
7. The producer and the transporter of the waste are required to comply with the legislation on waste, with the exception of the producer of the waste referred to in paragraph 3, letter b), who is required to comply only with the obligations provided for producers by the current legislation on waste. The manager of the integrated water service who, pursuant to paragraphs 3 and 5, treats waste is subject to the obligation to keep the loading and unloading register as provided for by the current legislation on waste.

**Art. 111**
**Aquaculture and fish farming plants**
1. By decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Agricultural and Forestry Policies, of Infrastructure and Transport, and of Productive Activities, and after agreement with the permanent Conference for relations between the State, the regions, and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, the criteria relating to the containment of the environmental impact deriving from aquaculture and fish farming activities are identified.

**Art. 112**
**Agronomic use**
1. Without prejudice to the provisions of Article 92 for vulnerable zones and of Legislative Decree No. 59 of 18 February 2005, for intensive livestock farming plants referred to in point 6.6 of ANNEX 1 to the aforementioned decree, the agronomic use of livestock effluents, of the vegetation water from olive mills, on the basis of the provisions of Law No. 574 of 11 November 1996, as well as of wastewater from the farms referred to in Article 101, paragraph 7, letters a), b), and c), and from small agri-food businesses, as identified by the decree of the Minister of Agricultural and Forestry Policies referred to in paragraph 2, is subject to communication to the competent authority pursuant to Article 75 of this decree.
2. The regions regulate the agronomic use activities referred to in paragraph 1 on the basis of the criteria and general technical standards adopted by decree of the Minister of Agricultural and Forestry Policies, in concert with the Ministers of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, of Productive Activities, of Health, and of Infrastructure and Transport, in agreement with the permanent Conference for relations between the State, the regions and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, within one hundred and eighty days from the date of entry into force of the aforementioned ministerial decree, while guaranteeing the protection of potentially affected water bodies and in particular the achievement or maintenance of the quality objectives referred to in the third part of this decree.
3. Within the framework of the regulations referred to in paragraph 2, the following are specifically regulated:
a) the methods of implementation of Articles 3, 5, 6, and 9 of Law No. 574 of 11 November 1996;
b) the times and methods for making the communication, providing for simplified procedures as well as specific cases of exemption from the obligation of communication for activities of minor environmental impact;
c) the technical standards for carrying out agronomic use operations;
d) the criteria and control procedures, including those relating to the imposition of prescriptions by the competent authority, the prohibition of exercise, or the temporary suspension of the activity referred to in paragraph 1 in case of non-communication or non-compliance with the technical standards and the prescriptions imposed;
e) the pecuniary administrative sanctions, without prejudice to the provisions of Article 137, paragraph 15.

**Art. 113**
**Stormwater runoff and first flush waters**
1. For the purposes of preventing hydraulic and environmental risks, the regions, after obtaining the opinion of the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, regulate and implement:
a) the forms of control of discharges of stormwater runoff from separate sewerage networks;
b) the cases in which it may be required that the discharge of stormwater runoff, carried out through other separate conduits, be subject to specific prescriptions, including possible authorization.
2. Stormwater not regulated pursuant to paragraph 1 is not subject to constraints or prescriptions deriving from the third part of this decree.
3. The regions also regulate the cases in which it may be required that first flush waters and waters for washing external areas be conveyed and appropriately treated in purification plants for particular conditions in which, in relation to the activities carried out, there is a risk of runoff from uncovered impermeable surfaces of hazardous substances or substances that create prejudice for the achievement of the quality objectives of the water bodies.
4. The discharge or direct release of stormwater into groundwater is in any case prohibited.

**Art. 114**
**Dams**
1. The regions, after obtaining the opinion of the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, shall adopt specific regulations concerning the restitution of water used for hydroelectric production, for irrigation purposes and in drinking water treatment plants, as well as water from surveys or drillings other than those related to the exploration and extraction of hydrocarbons, in order to ensure the maintenance or achievement of the quality objectives referred to in Title II of the third part of this decree.
2. In order to ensure the maintenance of the reservoir capacity and to safeguard both the quality of the impounded water and the receiving body, the desilting, flushing, and scouring operations of dams are carried out on the basis of a management plan for each reservoir. The management plan is aimed at defining both the forecast framework of said operations connected with the maintenance activities to be performed on the plant, and the prevention and protection measures for the receiving body, the aquatic ecosystem, fishing activities, and the water resources impounded and released downstream of the reservoir during the operations themselves.
3. The management plan also identifies any maneuvering methods of the discharge organs, also for the purpose of ensuring the protection of the receiving body. In any case, the provisions set by the Decree of the President of the Republic No. 1363 of 1 November 1959, aimed at guaranteeing the safety of people and property, remain valid.
4. The management plan is prepared by the operator on the basis of the criteria established by decree of the Minister of Infrastructure and Transport and of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities and with that of Agricultural and Forestry Policies, after agreement with the permanent Conference for relations between the State, the regions, and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, to be issued within one hundred and twenty days from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree.
5. The management plan is approved by the regions, with any prescriptions, within six months of its presentation, after obtaining the opinion of the administration responsible for supervising the safety of the reservoir and the dam, pursuant to Articles 89 and 91 of Legislative Decree No. 112 of 31 March 1998, and after consulting, where necessary, the managing bodies of the directly affected protected areas; for the dams referred to in the cited Article 91 of Legislative Decree No. 112 of 31 March 1998, the approved project is transmitted to the Italian Dams Register (RID) for insertion, also in synthetic form, as an integral part of the conditions sheet for the exercise and maintenance referred to in Article 6 of the Decree of the President of the Republic No. 1363 of 1 November 1959, and related implementing provisions. The management plan is considered approved and becomes operational six months after the date of presentation without any pronouncement from the competent region, without prejudice to the power of said Entities to issue any prescriptions, even after that deadline has passed.
6. With the approval of the project, the operator is authorized to carry out desilting, flushing, and scouring operations in accordance with the limits indicated in the project itself and with the related prescriptions.
7. In defining the concession fees for inert materials, the administrations shall determine specific methods and amounts to encourage the flushing and scouring of reservoirs by mechanical removal.
8. The operators of existing reservoirs, who have not yet complied with the obligations provided for by the decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea of 30 June 2004, published in the Official Gazette no. 269 of 16 November 2004, are required to present the project referred to in paragraph 2 within six months of the issuance of the decree referred to in paragraph 4. Until the approval or operation of the management project, and in any case no later than twelve months from the date of entry into force of the aforementioned decree, the periodic maneuvering operations prescribed pursuant to Article 17 of the Decree of the President of the Republic No. 1363 of 1 November 1959, aimed at checking the functionality of the discharge organs, are carried out in accordance with the condition sheets for exercise and maintenance.
9. The desilting, flushing, and scouring operations of the reservoirs must not prejudice the uses in progress downstream of the reservoir, nor the respect for the environmental quality objectives and the quality objectives for specific destination.

**Art. 115**
**Protection of areas appurtenant to water bodies**
1. In order to ensure the maintenance or restoration of spontaneous vegetation in the strip immediately adjacent to water bodies, with functions of filtering for suspended solids and pollutants of diffuse origin, of stabilizing the banks and of conserving biodiversity to be balanced with the needs of channel functionality, within one year from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree the regions regulate the interventions of transformation and management of the soil and subsoil provided for in the strip of at least 10 meters from the bank of rivers, lakes, ponds, and lagoons, in any case prohibiting the covering of watercourses that is not imposed by reasons of protection of public safety and the realization of waste disposal plants.
2. The interventions referred to in paragraph 1 are in any case subject to the authorization provided for by Royal Decree No. 523 of 25 July 1904, except as provided for interventions to safeguard public safety.
3. To guarantee the purposes of paragraph 1, the state-owned areas of rivers, torrents, lakes and other waters can be given in concession for the purpose of dedicating them to natural reserves, river or lake parks or in any case to restoration and environmental recovery interventions. If the state-owned areas are already included in state or regional protected natural areas included in the official list provided for by the current legislation, the concession is free of charge.
4. The areas of newly formed fluvial state property pursuant to Law No. 37 of 5 January 1994, cannot be subject to de-accession from state property.

**Art. 116**
**Programs of measures**
1. The regions, within the limits of available resources, shall integrate the Protection Plans referred to in Article 121 with the programs of measures consisting of the basic measures referred to in Annex 11 to the third part of this decree and, where necessary, of the supplementary measures referred to in the same Annex; these programs of measures are submitted for approval to the Basin Authority. If the measures are not sufficient to guarantee the achievement of the planned objectives, the Basin Authority shall identify the causes and indicate to the regions the methods for reviewing the programs, inviting them to make the necessary changes, without prejudice to the limit constituted by the available resources. The basic and supplementary measures must in any case be such as to avoid any increase in pollution of marine and surface waters. The programs are approved by 2009 and implemented by the regions by 2012; the subsequent review must take place by 2015 and must be updated every six years.

**TITLE IV - INSTRUMENTS OF PROTECTION**

**CHAPTER I - MANAGEMENT PLANS AND WATER PROTECTION PLANS**

**Art. 117**
**Management plans and register of protected areas**
1. For each hydrographic district, a Management Plan is adopted, which represents an internal articulation of the district basin plan referred to in Article 65. The Management Plan therefore constitutes a sectoral plan of the basin plan and is adopted and approved according to the procedures established for the latter by Article 66. The Basin Authorities, for the purposes of preparing the Management Plans, must guarantee the participation of all competent institutional subjects in the specific sector.
2. The Management Plan is composed of the elements indicated in part A of Annex 4 to the third part of this decree.
3. The Basin Authority, having heard the Area Authorities of the integrated water service, establishes within six months from the date of entry into force of this regulation, on the basis of the information transmitted by the regions, a register of the protected areas referred to in Annex 9 to the third part of this decree, designated by the competent authorities pursuant to the current legislation.

**Art. 118**
**Survey of the characteristics of the river basin and analysis of the impact exerted by anthropic activity**
1. In order to update the information necessary for the drafting of the Protection Plan referred to in Article 121, the regions shall implement specific data survey programs useful for describing the characteristics of the river basin and for evaluating the anthropic impact exerted on it, as well as for the collection of the data necessary for the economic analysis of the use of water, as provided for in Annex 10 to the third part of this decree. The results of the above activities are transmitted to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and to the Department for the protection of inland and marine waters of the Agency for Environmental Protection and for Technical Services (APAT).
2. The programs referred to in paragraph 1 are adopted in accordance with the indications of Annex 3 to the third part of this decree and with the provisions adopted by a specific decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and are updated every six years.
3. In carrying out the cognitive activity referred to in paragraph 1, the regions are required to use the data and information already acquired.

**Art. 119**
**Principle of cost recovery for water services**
1. For the purpose of achieving the quality objectives of Chapter I of Title II of the third part of this decree, the competent Authorities shall take into account the principle of cost recovery of water services, including environmental and resource-related ones, taking into consideration the economic analysis carried out on the basis of Annex 10 to the third part of this decree and, in particular, according to the "polluter pays" principle.
2. By 2010, the competent Authorities shall implement water pricing policies suitable to adequately incentivize users to use water resources efficiently and to contribute to the achievement and maintenance of the environmental quality objectives referred to in Directive 2000/60/EC as well as in Articles 76 and following of this decree, including through an adequate contribution to the cost recovery of water services from the various water use sectors, divided at least into industry, households, and agriculture. In this regard, the social, environmental, and economic repercussions of the recovery of the aforementioned costs, as well as the geographical and climatic conditions of the region or regions in question, must in any case be taken into account. In particular:
a) the concession fees for the derivations of public waters shall take into account the environmental costs and the resource costs associated with the use of water;
b) the tariffs of water services charged to the various water use sectors, such as civil, industrial, and agricultural, shall contribute adequately to the cost recovery on the basis of the economic analysis carried out according to Annex 10 to the third part of this decree.
3. In the Protection Plans referred to in Article 121, the phases planned for the implementation of the provisions of paragraphs 1 and 2 necessary for the achievement of the quality objectives of the third part of this decree are reported.

**Art. 120**
**Survey of the quality status of water bodies**
1. The regions shall prepare and implement programs for the knowledge and verification of the qualitative and quantitative status of surface and groundwater within each river basin.
2. The programs referred to in paragraph 1 are adopted in accordance with the indications of Annex 1 to the third part of this decree. These programs must be integrated with those already existing for the objectives for specific destination established in accordance with Annex 2 to the third part of this decree, as well as with those of the waters included in the register of protected areas. The results of the activities referred to in paragraph 1 are transmitted to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and to the Department for the protection of inland and marine waters of the Agency for Environmental Protection and for Technical Services (APAT).
3. In order to avoid overlaps and to guarantee the flow of the information collected and its compatibility with the National Environmental Information System (SINA), the regions may promote, in the exercise of their respective competencies, program agreements with the Agency for Environmental Protection and for Technical Services (APAT), the regional agencies for environmental protection referred to in decree-law no. 496 of 4 December 1993, converted, with modifications, by law no. 61 of 21 January 1994, the provinces, the Area Authorities, the consortia for land reclamation and irrigation, and the other interested public bodies. The programs must also define the methods for data standardization and information exchange.

**Art. 121**
**Water protection plans**
1. The Water Protection Plan constitutes a specific sectoral plan and is articulated according to the contents listed in this article, as well as according to the specifications indicated in part B of Annex 4 to the third part of this decree.
2. By 31 December 2006, the Basin Authorities, in the context of planning activities or through specific acts of guidance and coordination, having heard the provinces and the Area Authorities, shall define the objectives on a district scale to which the water protection plans must adhere, as well as the priorities of the interventions. By 31 December 2007, the regions, having heard the provinces and after adopting any safeguard measures, shall adopt the Water Protection Plan and transmit it to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea as well as to the competent Basin Authorities, for verification of competence.
3. The Protection Plan contains, in addition to the interventions aimed at guaranteeing the achievement or maintenance of the objectives referred to in the third part of this decree, the necessary measures for the qualitative and quantitative protection of the water system.
4. For the purposes of paragraph 1, the Protection Plan contains in particular:
a) the results of the cognitive activity;
b) the identification of the environmental quality objectives and for specific destination;
c) the list of water bodies for specific destination and of the areas requiring specific measures for the prevention of pollution and for remediation;
d) the qualitative and quantitative protection measures, integrated and coordinated among themselves by river basin;
e) the indication of the temporal frequency of the interventions and their relative priorities;
f) the program for verifying the effectiveness of the planned interventions;
g) the remediation interventions of the water bodies;
h) the economic analysis referred to in Annex 10 to the third part of this decree and the measures planned in order to implement the provisions of Article 119 concerning the cost recovery of water services;
i) the financial resources provided for by the current legislation.
5. Within one hundred and twenty days of the transmission of the Protection Plan, the Basin Authorities shall verify the conformity of the plan with the planning acts or with the acts of guidance and coordination referred to in paragraph 2, expressing a binding opinion. The Protection Plan is approved by the regions within the subsequent six months and in any case no later than 31 December 2008. The subsequent revisions and updates must be carried out every six years.

**Art. 122**
**Public information and consultation**
1. The regions promote the active participation of all interested parties in the implementation of the third part of this decree, in particular in the elaboration, review, and updating of the Protection Plans. Upon motivated request, the regions authorize access to the reference documents and information on the basis of which the draft of the Protection Plan was prepared. The regions shall ensure that, for the territory of competence falling within the respective hydrographic district, the following are published and made available for any observations by the public:
a) the calendar and work program for the presentation of the Plan, including a declaration of the consultative measures to be taken at least three years before the start of the period to which the Plan refers;
b) a provisional global assessment of the priority problems for the management of water within the respective hydrographic basin, at least two years before the start of the period to which the Plan refers;
c) a copy of the draft Protection Plan, at least one year before the start of the period to which the plan refers.
2. To guarantee active participation and consultation, the regions shall grant a minimum period of six months for the presentation of written observations on the documents referred to in paragraph 1.
3. Paragraphs 1 and 2 also apply to the updates of the Protection Plans.

**Art. 123**
**Transmission of information and reports**
1. Concurrently with the publication of the Protection Plans, the regions shall transmit a copy of said plans and all subsequent updates to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea for the purpose of their subsequent forwarding to the European Commission.
2. The regions shall transmit to the same Ministry for subsequent forwarding to the European Commission, also on the basis of the information dictated, in the matter of methods for transmitting information on the quality status of water bodies and on the classification of waters, by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea with a specific decree, summary reports concerning:
a) the cognitive activity referred to in Article 118 within twelve months from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree. The subsequent updates are transmitted every six years starting from February 2010;
b) the monitoring programs according to the provisions of Article 120 within twelve months from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree and subsequently on an annual basis.
3. Within three years of the publication of each Protection Plan or of the update referred to in Article 121, the regions shall transmit to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea a report on the progress made in the implementation of the basic or supplementary measures referred to in Article 116.

**CHAPTER II - AUTHORIZATION OF DISCHARGES**

**Art. 124**
**General criteria**
1. All discharges must be preventively authorized.
2. The authorization is issued to the holder of the activity from which the discharge originates. Where one or more establishments discharge to a third party, the holder of the final discharge, the wastewater from their activities, or where a consortium is established between several establishments for the joint discharge of wastewater from the activities of the consortium members, the authorization is issued to the holder of the final discharge or to the consortium itself, without prejudice to the responsibilities of the individual holders of the aforementioned activities and of the manager of the related purification plant in case of violation of the provisions of the third part of this decree. Where one or more establishments make discharges in common without having formed a consortium, the discharge authorization is issued to the holder of the final discharge, it being understood that the issuance of the authorization or its renewal is subject to the approval of a suitable project demonstrating the technical possibility of partitioning the individual discharges.
3. The authorization regime for discharges of domestic wastewater and from sewerage networks, whether or not served by urban wastewater treatment plants, is defined by the regions within the framework of the discipline referred to in Article 101, paragraphs 1 and 2.
4. By way of derogation from paragraph 1, discharges of domestic wastewater into sewerage networks are always permitted in compliance with the regulations established by the manager of the integrated water service and approved by the Area Authority.
5. The authorization regime for discharges of thermal wastewater is defined by the regions; such discharges are permitted in sewerage networks in compliance with the regulations issued by the manager of the integrated water service and in accordance with the authorization issued by the Area Authority.
6. The regions regulate the phases of provisional authorization for the discharges of wastewater treatment plants for the time necessary for their start-up.
7. Unless otherwise provided by regional regulations, the application for authorization is submitted to the province or to the Area Authority if the discharge is into a public sewer system. The competent authority shall provide a decision within sixty days of receiving the application. If said authority is non-compliant within the terms indicated above, the authorization is considered temporarily granted for the subsequent sixty days, subject to revocation.
8. Without prejudice to the provisions of Legislative Decree No. 59 of 18 February 2005, the authorization is valid for four years from the moment of its issuance. A renewal must be requested one year before its expiry. The discharge may be provisionally maintained in operation in compliance with the prescriptions contained in the previous authorization, until the adoption of a new provision, if the renewal application has been submitted in a timely manner. For discharges containing hazardous substances referred to in Article 108, the renewal must be granted explicitly within and no later than six months from the expiry date; once this term has passed without effect, the discharge must cease immediately. The regional discipline referred to in paragraph 3 may provide for specific types of discharges of domestic wastewater, where subject to authorization, forms of tacit renewal of the same.
9. For discharges into a watercourse where a natural null flow is ascertained for more than one hundred and twenty days a year, or into a non-significant water body, the authorization takes into account the period of null flow and the dilution capacity of the water body in other periods, and establishes prescriptions and limits in order to guarantee the self-purification capacities of the receiving body and the protection of groundwater.
10. In relation to the technical characteristics of the discharge, its location, and the local conditions of the interested environment, the authorization contains further technical prescriptions aimed at ensuring that the discharge, including the operations functionally connected to it, occurs in accordance with the provisions of the third part of this decree and without any prejudice to the receiving body, public health, and the environment.
11. The expenses necessary for carrying out surveys, checks, controls, and inspections necessary for the preliminary investigation of the applications for discharge authorization provided for by the third part of this decree are borne by the applicant. The competent authority determines, prior to the preliminary investigation and on a provisional basis, the sum that the applicant is required to pay, as a deposit, as a condition for the admissibility of the application. The same Authority, once the preliminary investigation is completed, shall proceed with the final settlement of the expenses incurred on the basis of a tariff prepared by it.
12. For settlements, buildings, or establishments whose activity is transferred to another location, or for those subject to a different use, expansion, or restructuring from which a discharge derives with qualitatively and/or quantitatively different characteristics from that of the pre-existing discharge, a new authorization for the discharge must be requested, if the latter is subject to it. In cases where the discharge does not have different qualitative or quantitative characteristics, communication must be given to the competent authority, which, having verified the compatibility of the discharge with the receiving body, shall adopt the measures that may become necessary.

**Art. 125**
**Application for authorization of industrial wastewater discharges**
1. The application for authorization of industrial wastewater discharges must be accompanied by the indication of the quantitative and qualitative characteristics of the discharge and the annual volume of water to be discharged, the type of receiver, the identification of the point planned for carrying out control samples, the description of the overall discharge system including the operations functionally connected to it, any system for measuring the flow of discharges, where required, and the indication of the equipment used in the production process and in the discharge systems as well as the purification systems used to achieve compliance with the emission limit values.
2. In the case of discharges of substances referred to in table 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, deriving from the production cycles indicated in the same table 3/A, the application referred to in paragraph 1 must also indicate:
a) the production capacity of the individual industrial establishment that involves the production or transformation or use of the substances referred to in the same table, or the presence of such substances in the discharge. The production capacity must be indicated with reference to the maximum hourly capacity multiplied by the maximum number of daily working hours and by the maximum number of working days;
b) the hourly water requirement for each specific production process.

**Art. 126**
**Approval of the projects of urban wastewater treatment plants**
1. The regions regulate the approval procedures for the projects of urban wastewater treatment plants. This discipline must take into account the criteria of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree and the correspondence between the treatment capacity of the plant and the needs of the areas served, as well as the management methods that must ensure compliance with the discharge limit values. The regions also regulate the provisional authorization procedures necessary for the start-up of the plant, including in the case of construction in functional lots.

**Art. 127**
**Sludge from the treatment of wastewater**
1. Without prejudice to the discipline of Legislative Decree No. 99 of 27 January 1992, the sludge deriving from the treatment of wastewater is subject to the discipline of waste, where applicable. The sludge must be reused whenever its reuse is appropriate.
2. The disposal of sludge in fresh and brackish surface waters is prohibited.

**CHAPTER III - CONTROL OF DISCHARGES**

**Art. 128**
**Subjects required to control**
5. The competent authority carries out the control of discharges on the basis of a program that ensures a periodic, widespread, effective, and impartial system of controls.
6. Without prejudice to what is established in paragraph 1, for discharges into public sewers the manager of the integrated water service organizes an adequate control service according to the methods provided for in the management agreement.

**Art. 129**
**Access and inspections**
1. The authority competent for control is authorized to carry out the inspections, controls, and samples necessary to ascertain compliance with the emission limit values, the prescriptions contained in the authorizing or regulatory provisions, and the conditions that give rise to the formation of the discharges. The holder of the discharge is required to provide the information requested and to allow access to the places from which the discharge originates.

**Art. 130**
**Non-compliance with the prescriptions of the discharge authorization**
1. Without prejudice to the application of the sanctioning norms of Title V of the third part of this decree, in case of non-compliance with the prescriptions of the discharge authorization, the competent authority proceeds, according to the gravity of the infraction:
a) with a warning, establishing a term within which the non-compliances must be eliminated;
b) with a warning and simultaneous suspension of the authorization for a specified period, if situations of danger to public health and the environment arise;
c) with the revocation of the authorization in case of failure to adapt to the prescriptions imposed with the warning and in case of repeated violations that determine a situation of danger to public health and the environment.

**Art. 131**
**Control of discharges of hazardous substances**
1. For discharges containing the substances referred to in Table 5 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, the authority competent for issuing the authorization may prescribe, at the expense of the holder of the discharge, the installation of automatic control instruments, as well as the methods for their management and for the conservation of the relative results, which must remain available to the authority competent for control for a period of not less than three years from the date of execution of the individual controls.

**Art. 132**
**Substitute interventions**
1. In the case of failure to carry out the controls provided for by the third part of this decree, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall warn the region to provide within the maximum term of one hundred and eighty days or within the shorter term imposed by the needs of environmental protection. In case of persistent non-compliance, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall provide, in a substitute capacity, after deliberation of the Council of Ministers, with charges borne by the non-compliant Entity.
2. In the exercise of the substitute powers referred to in paragraph 1, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall appoint an "ad acta" commissioner who carries out the acts necessary for the fulfillments provided for by the current legislation at the expense of the regions for the purpose of organizing the control system.

**TITLE V - SANCTIONS**

**CHAPTER I - ADMINISTRATIVE SANCTIONS**

**Art. 133**
**Administrative sanctions**
1. Anyone who, unless the act constitutes a crime, in carrying out a discharge exceeds the emission limit values set in the tables of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, or the different limit values established by the regions according to Article 101, paragraph 2, or those set by the competent authority according to Article 107, paragraph 1, or Article 108, paragraph 1, is punished with an administrative sanction from three thousand euros to thirty thousand euros. If the non-compliance with the limit values concerns discharges into the safeguard areas of water resources intended for human consumption referred to in Article 94, or into water bodies located in the protected areas referred to in the current legislation, an administrative sanction of not less than twenty thousand euros is applied.
2. Anyone who opens or in any way carries out discharges of domestic wastewater or from sewerage networks, whether or not served by public purification plants, without the authorization referred to in Article 124, or continues to carry out or maintain said discharges after the authorization has been suspended or revoked, is punished with an administrative sanction from six thousand euros to sixty thousand euros. In the case of discharges related to isolated buildings used for residential purposes, the sanction is from six hundred euros to three thousand euros.
3. Anyone who, unless the act constitutes a crime, outside the cases referred to in paragraph 1, carries out or maintains a discharge without observing the prescriptions indicated in the authorization provision or set pursuant to Article 107, paragraph 1, is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from one thousand five hundred euros to fifteen thousand euros.
4. Anyone who, unless the act constitutes a crime, carries out the dumping at sea of the materials indicated in Article 109, paragraph 1, letters a) and b), or carries out the activity of laying at sea referred to in paragraph 5 of the same article, without authorization, is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from one thousand five hundred euros to fifteen thousand euros.
5. Unless the act constitutes a crime, until the issuance of the regional discipline referred to in Article 112, paragraph 2, anyone who does not observe the provisions of Article 170, paragraph 7, is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from six hundred euros to six thousand euros.
6. Anyone who, unless the act constitutes a crime, does not observe the prohibition of disposal of sludge provided for by Article 127, paragraph 2, is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from six thousand euros to sixty thousand euros.
7. Unless the act constitutes a crime, anyone who:
a) in carrying out the operations of desilting, flushing, or scouring of dams, exceeds the limits or does not observe the other prescriptions contained in the specific management project of the plant referred to in Article 114, paragraph 2;
b) carries out the same operations before the approval of the management project.
is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from three thousand euros to thirty thousand euros.
8. Anyone who violates the prescriptions concerning the installation and maintenance of devices for measuring flow rates and volumes, or the obligation to transmit the results of the measurements referred to in Article 95, paragraph 3, is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from one thousand five hundred euros to six thousand euros. In cases of particular triviality, the sanction is reduced to one-fifth.
9. Anyone who does not comply with the discipline laid down by the regions pursuant to Article 113, paragraph 1, letter b), is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from one thousand five hundred euros to fifteen thousand euros.

**Art. 134**
**Sanctions regarding safeguard areas**
1. Non-compliance with the provisions relating to the activities and destinations prohibited in the safeguard areas referred to in Article 94 is punished with a pecuniary administrative sanction from six hundred euros to six thousand euros.

**Art. 135**
**Competence and jurisdiction**
1. Regarding the ascertainment of administrative offenses, the region or the autonomous province in whose territory the violation was committed shall provide for the imposition of pecuniary administrative sanctions, by means of an order-injunction pursuant to Articles 18 and following of Law No. 689 of 24 November 1981, with the exception of the sanctions provided for in Article 133, paragraph 8, for which the municipality is competent, without prejudice to the attributions assigned by law to other public authorities.
2. Without prejudice to the provisions of Legislative Decree No. 112 of 31 March 1998, for the purposes of surveillance and ascertainment of offenses in violation of the norms on the protection of waters from pollution, the Carabinieri Command for the protection of the environment (C.C.T.A.) shall act; the State Forestry Corps may also intervene, and the Guardia di Finanza and the State Police may contribute. The Corps of the port authorities, Coast Guard, shall provide for the surveillance and ascertainment of the violations of the third part of this decree when damage or situations of danger to the marine and coastal environment may derive from them.
3. For criminal proceedings pending upon the entry into force of the third part of this decree, the judicial authority, if it does not have to issue a decree of dismissal or a sentence of acquittal, shall order the transmission of the acts to the entities indicated in paragraph 1 for the purposes of applying the administrative sanctions.
4. The payment in a reduced measure referred to in Article 16 of Law No. 689 of 24 November 1981 does not apply to the pecuniary administrative sanctions provided for by the third part of this decree.

**Art. 136**
**Proceeds from pecuniary administrative sanctions**
1. The sums deriving from the proceeds of the administrative sanctions provided for by the third part of this decree are paid to the entry of the regional budget to be reassigned to the basic forecast units intended for the works of remediation and reduction of pollution of water bodies. The regions shall provide for the distribution of the sums collected among the prevention and remediation interventions.

**CHAPTER II - PENAL SANCTIONS**

**Art. 137**
**Penal sanctions**
1. Anyone who opens or in any way carries out new discharges of industrial wastewater, without authorization, or continues to carry out or maintain said discharges after the authorization has been suspended or revoked, is punished with arrest from two months to two years or with a fine from one thousand five hundred euros to ten thousand euros.
2. When the conducts described in paragraph 1 concern discharges of industrial wastewater containing the hazardous substances included in the families and groups of substances indicated in tables 5 and 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, the penalty is arrest from three months to three years.
3. Anyone who, outside the cases referred to in paragraph 5, carries out a discharge of industrial wastewater containing the hazardous substances included in the families and groups of substances indicated in tables 5 and 3/A of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree without observing the prescriptions of the authorization, or the other prescriptions of the competent authority under Articles 107, paragraph 1, and 108, paragraph 4, is punished with arrest up to two years.
4. Anyone who violates the prescriptions concerning the installation and management of automatic controls or the obligation to preserve their results, as per Article 131, is punished with the penalty of paragraph 3.
5. Anyone who, in carrying out a discharge of industrial wastewater, exceeds the limit values set in table 3 or, in the case of discharge on the soil, in table 4 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, or exceeds the more restrictive limits set by the regions or autonomous provinces or by the competent Authority under Article 107, paragraph 1, in relation to the substances indicated in table 5 of Annex 5 to the third part of this decree, is punished with arrest up to two years and with a fine from three thousand euros to thirty thousand euros. If the limit values set for the substances contained in table 3/A of the same Annex 5 are also exceeded, arrest from six months to three years and a fine from six thousand euros to one hundred and twenty thousand euros apply.
6. The sanctions referred to in paragraph 5 also apply to the manager of urban wastewater treatment plants who, in carrying out the discharge, exceeds the limit values provided for by the same paragraph.
7. The manager of the integrated water service who does not comply with the communication obligation of Article 110, paragraph 3, or does not observe the prescriptions or prohibitions of Article 110, paragraph 5, is punished with arrest from three months to one year or with a fine from three thousand euros to thirty thousand euros if it concerns non-hazardous waste, and with the penalty of arrest from six months to two years and with a fine from three thousand euros to thirty thousand euros if it concerns hazardous waste.
8. The holder of a discharge who does not allow access to the settlements by the person in charge of control for the purposes of Article 101, paragraphs 3 and 4, unless the act constitutes a more serious crime, is punished with the penalty of arrest up to two years. The powers-duties of intervention of the persons in charge of control, also pursuant to Article 13 of Law no. 689 of 1981 and Articles 55 and 354 of the code of criminal procedure, remain firm.
9. Anyone who does not comply with the discipline laid down by the regions pursuant to Article 113, paragraph 3, is punished with the sanctions of Article 137, paragraph 1.
10. Anyone who does not comply with the measure adopted by the competent authority pursuant to Article 84, paragraph 4, or Article 85, paragraph 2, is punished with a fine from one thousand five hundred euros to fifteen thousand euros.
11. Anyone who does not observe the discharge prohibitions provided for by Articles 103 and 104 is punished with arrest up to three years.
12. Anyone who does not observe the regional prescriptions adopted under Article 88, paragraphs 1 and 2, aimed at ensuring the achievement or restoration of the quality objectives of the waters designated pursuant to Article 87, or does not comply with the measures adopted by the competent authority pursuant to Article 87, paragraph 3, is punished with arrest up to two years or with a fine from four thousand euros to forty thousand euros.
13. The penalty of arrest from two months to two years is always applied if the discharge into the waters of the sea from ships or aircraft contains substances or materials for which the absolute prohibition of dumping is imposed under the provisions contained in the international conventions in force on the matter and ratified by Italy, unless they are in quantities such as to be rendered rapidly harmless by the physical, chemical, and biological processes that occur naturally in the sea and provided that there is prior authorization from the competent authority.
14. Anyone who carries out the agronomic use of livestock effluents, vegetation water from olive mills, as well as wastewater from agricultural and small agri-food businesses as per Article 112, outside the cases and procedures provided therein, or does not comply with the prohibition or order of suspension of the activity issued under said article, is punished with a fine from one thousand five hundred euros to ten thousand euros or with arrest up to one year. The same penalty applies to anyone who carries out agronomic use outside the cases and procedures of the current legislation.

**Art. 138**
**Further sanctioning measures for shellfish farming activity**
1. In the cases provided for by paragraph 12 of Article 137, the Minister of Health, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, as well as the competent region and autonomous province, to whom a copy of the criminal reports is sent, may order, for their respective competencies and regardless of the outcome of the criminal trial, the precautionary suspension of the shellfish farming activity; following a sentence of conviction or a decision issued pursuant to Article 444 of the code of criminal procedure that have become final, they may also order, having assessed the gravity of the facts, the closure of the plants.

**Art. 139**
**Obligations of the convicted person**
1. With the sentence of conviction for the crimes provided for in the third part of this decree, or with the decision issued pursuant to Article 444 of the code of criminal procedure, the benefit of the conditional suspension of the penalty may be subordinated to the compensation for the damage and to the execution of the safety, remediation, and restoration interventions.

**Art. 140**
**Attenuating circumstance**
1. Towards those who, before the criminal judgment or the order-injunction, have fully repaired the damage, the penal and administrative sanctions provided for in this title are reduced from one half to two thirds.

**SECTION III - MANAGEMENT OF WATER RESOURCES**

**TITLE I - GENERAL PRINCIPLES AND COMPETENCIES**

**Art. 141**
**Scope of application**
1. The subject of the provisions contained in this section is the discipline of the management of water resources and of the integrated water service for the profiles concerning the protection of the environment and competition and the determination of the essential levels of the performances of the integrated water service and of the related fundamental functions of municipalities, provinces and metropolitan cities.
2. The integrated water service consists of the set of public services of capture, adduction and distribution of water for civil uses, of sewerage and of purification of wastewater, and must be managed according to principles of efficiency, effectiveness and economy, in compliance with national and community norms. These provisions also apply to the industrial uses of water managed within the integrated water service.

**Art. 142**
**Competencies**
1. Within the framework of the competencies defined by the constitutional norms, and without prejudice to the competencies of the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea exercises the functions and tasks pertaining to the State in the matters regulated by this section.
2. The regions exercise the functions and tasks pertaining to them within the framework of the constitutionally determined competencies and in respect of the state attributions of paragraph 1, and in particular they provide for the governance of their respective territory.
3. Local authorities, through the Area Authority of Article 148, paragraph 1, carry out the functions of organizing the integrated water service, of choosing the form of management, of determining and modulating the tariffs for users, of entrusting the management and its related control, according to the provisions of the third part of this decree.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 143**
**Ownership of infrastructures**
1. Aqueducts, sewers, purification plants and other public-owned water infrastructures, up to the point of delivery and/or measurement, are part of the state property pursuant to Articles 822 and following of the civil code and are inalienable except in the ways and within the limits established by law.
2. The Area Authority is also responsible for the protection of the assets referred to in paragraph 1, pursuant to Article 823, second paragraph, of the civil code.

**Art. 144**
**Protection and use of water resources**
1. All surface and groundwater, even if not extracted from the subsoil, belong to the State property.
2. Water constitutes a resource that must be protected and used according to criteria of solidarity; any use of it is carried out safeguarding the expectations and rights of future generations to enjoy an intact environmental heritage.
3. The discipline of the uses of water is aimed at their rationalization, in order to avoid waste and to favor the renewal of resources, not to prejudice the water heritage, the livability of the environment, agriculture, fish farming, aquatic fauna and flora, geomorphological processes and hydrological balances.
4. Uses other than human consumption are permitted within the limits in which the water resources are sufficient and on condition that they do not prejudice their quality.
5. Thermal, mineral and geothermal waters are regulated by specific norms, in respect of the division of constitutionally determined competencies.

**Art. 145**
**Equilibrium of the water balance**
1.
