The competent Basin Authority defines and periodically updates the water balance aimed at ensuring the equilibrium between the availability of resources that can be sourced or activated in the reference area and the needs for the different uses, in respect of the criteria and objectives of Article 144.
2. To ensure the equilibrium between resources and needs, the competent Basin Authority adopts, for its competence, the measures for the planning of the water economy in function of the uses for which the resources are intended.
3. In river basins characterized by substantial withdrawals or transfers, both downstream and beyond the watershed line, the derivations are regulated in such a way as to guarantee the necessary flow level for life in the underlying riverbeds and such as not to damage the equilibria of the interested ecosystems.

**Art. 146**
**Water saving**
1. Within one year from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, the regions, having heard the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), in respect of the principles of state legislation, shall adopt norms and measures aimed at rationalizing consumption and eliminating waste and in particular at:
a) improving the maintenance of the adduction and distribution networks of water for any use intended to reduce losses;
b) providing, in the construction or replacement of new transport and distribution plants for water, both internal and external, the obligation to use anti-corrosion protection systems for metal pipelines;
c) realizing, in particular in new residential, commercial and productive settlements of significant size, dual adduction networks for the purpose of using less valuable water for compatible uses;
d) promoting information and the dissemination of methods and techniques of domestic water saving and in the industrial, tertiary and agricultural sectors;
e) adopting high-efficiency irrigation systems accompanied by their correct management and by the replacement, where appropriate, of open channel networks with pressurized networks;
f) installing meters for the consumption of water in each single housing unit as well as differentiated meters for the productive activities and the tertiary sector carried out in the urban context;
g) realizing in new settlements, when economically and technically convenient also in relation to the final receiving bodies, differentiated collection systems for rainwater and for wastewater and first flush;
h) identifying aquifer recharge areas and adopting protection and management measures aimed at guaranteeing a quantitatively and qualitatively suitable recharge process.
2. Urban planning instruments, compatibly with the urban and territorial structure and with the available financial resources, must provide for dual networks for the purpose of making possible appropriate uses of even non-potable water. The issuance of the building permit is subordinated to the provision, in the project, of the installation of meters for each single housing unit, as well as of the connection to dual networks, where already available.
3. Within one year from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, having heard the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and the Department for the protection of inland and marine waters of the Agency for Environmental Protection and for Technical Services (APAT), shall adopt a regulation for the definition of the criteria and methods on the basis of which to evaluate the losses of aqueducts and sewers. By the month of February of each year, the managers of the water services shall transmit to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and to the competent Area Authority the results of the surveys carried out with the aforesaid methods.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**TITLE II - INTEGRATED WATER SERVICE**

**Art. 147**
**Territorial organization of the integrated water service**
1. The water services are organized on the basis of the optimal territorial areas defined by the regions in implementation of Law No. 36 of 5 January 1994.
2. The regions may modify the delimitations of the optimal territorial areas to improve the management of the integrated water service, in any case ensuring its performance according to criteria of efficiency, effectiveness and economy, in respect, in particular, of the following principles:
a) unity of the river basin or of the sub-basin or of the contiguous river basins, taking into account the basin plans, as well as the location of the resources and their constraints of destination, also deriving from custom, in favor of the interested inhabited centers;
b) uniqueness of the management and, in any case, overcoming of the vertical fragmentation of the managements;
c) adequacy of the management dimensions, defined on the basis of physical, demographic, technical parameters.
3. The regions, having heard the provinces, shall establish supplementary norms for the control of the discharges of civil and productive settlements connected to public sewers, for the functionality of pretreatment plants and for compliance with the limits and prescriptions provided for by the relative authorizations.

**Art. 148**
**Optimal territorial area authority**
1. The Area Authority is a structure with legal personality established in each optimal territorial area delimited by the competent region, in which the local authorities mandatorily participate and to which the exercise of the competencies pertaining to them in the matter of management of water resources is transferred, including the programming of the water infrastructures referred to in Article 143, paragraph 1.
2. The regions and autonomous provinces may regulate the forms and ways of cooperation between the local authorities falling within the same optimal area, providing that they themselves constitute the Area Authorities referred to in paragraph 1, to which the organization, entrustment and control of the management of the integrated water service is delegated.
3. The preventive and final budgets of the Area Authority and their variations are published by posting on a special notice board, established at the headquarters of the body, and are transmitted to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea within fifteen days of the adoption of the relative resolutions.
4. The operating costs of the operational structure of the Area Authority, determined annually, are charged to the local authorities falling within the optimal territorial area, based on the participation quotas of each of them in the Area Authority.
5. Without prejudice to the mandatory participation in the Area Authority of all local authorities pursuant to paragraph 1, adhesion to the single management of the integrated water service is optional for municipalities with a population of up to 1,000 inhabitants included in the territory of the mountain communities, on condition that the management of the water service is operated directly by the municipal administration or through a company with entirely public capital and controlled by the same municipality. On the managements of this paragraph, the Area Authority exercises functions of general regulation and control. With a specific service contract stipulated with the Area Authority, after a program agreement, criteria and methods are defined for the eventual participation in initiatives promoted by the Area Authority itself.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 149**
**Area plan**
1. Within twelve months from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, the Area Authority shall provide for the preparation and/or updating of the area plan. The area plan consists of the following acts:
a) survey of the infrastructures;
b) program of interventions;
c) management and organizational model;
d) economic and financial plan.
2. The survey, also on the basis of information certified by the local authorities falling within the optimal territorial area, identifies the state of consistency of the infrastructures to be entrusted to the manager of the integrated water service, specifying their state of operation.
3. The program of interventions identifies the extraordinary maintenance works and the new works to be carried out, including the interventions for the adaptation of already existing infrastructures, necessary to achieve at least the minimum service levels, as well as to satisfy the overall demand of the users. The program of interventions, commensurate with the entire management, specifies the objectives to be achieved, indicating the infrastructures planned for this purpose and the implementation times.
4. The economic and financial plan, articulated in the balance sheet, the income statement, and the cash flow statement, provides, on an annual basis, the trend of the management and investment costs net of any public funding grants. It is integrated by the annual forecast of the revenues from tariffs, extended to the entire period of entrustment. The plan, as drafted, must guarantee the achievement of the economic and financial equilibrium and, in any case, respect for the principles of effectiveness, efficiency, and economy of the management, also in relation to the planned investments.
5. The management and organizational model defines the operational structure through which the manager ensures the service to the users and the realization of the program of interventions.
6. The area plan is transmitted within ten days of the approval resolution to the competent region, to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea. The Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) may notify the Area Authority, within ninety days from the receipt of the plan, its findings or observations, dictating, where necessary, prescriptions concerning: the program of interventions, with particular reference to the adequacy of the planned investments in relation to the minimum service levels identified as management objectives; the financial plan, with particular reference to the capacity of the tariff evolution to guarantee the economic and financial equilibrium of the management, also in relation to the planned investments.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 150**
**Choice of the form of management and entrustment procedures**
1. The Area Authority, in respect of the area plan and the principle of uniqueness of management for each area, deliberates the form of management from among those of Article 113, paragraph 5, of Legislative Decree No. 267 of 18 August 2000.
2. The Area Authority awards the management of the integrated water service by means of a tender regulated by the principles and community provisions, in accordance with the criteria of Article 113, paragraph 7, of Legislative Decree No. 267 of 18 August 2000, according to methods and terms established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in respect of regional competencies on the matter.
3. The management can also be entrusted to companies participated in exclusively and directly by municipalities or other local authorities included in the optimal territorial area, if objective technical or economic reasons exist, according to the provision of paragraph 5, letter c), of Article 113 of Legislative Decree No. 267 of 18 August 2000, or to companies only partially participated in by such entities, according to the provision of paragraph 5, letter b), of Article 113 of Legislative Decree No. 267 of 18 August 2000, provided that the private partner has been chosen, before the entrustment, with a tender to be carried out with the methods of paragraph 2.
4. The subjects of this article manage the integrated water service over the entire territory of the local authorities falling within the optimal territorial area, except as provided for in Article 148, paragraph 5.

**Art. 151**
**Relations between area authorities and managers of the integrated water service**
1. The relations between Area Authorities and managers of the integrated water service are regulated by conventions prepared by the Area Authority.
2. To this end, the regions and autonomous provinces adopt standard conventions, with related specifications, which must provide in particular:
a) the legal regime chosen for the management of the service;
b) the duration of the entrustment, not exceeding in any case thirty years;
c) the obligation to achieve the economic and financial equilibrium of the management;
d) the level of efficiency and reliability of the service to be assured to the users, also with reference to the maintenance of the plants;
e) the criteria and methods of application of the tariffs determined by the Area Authority and their annual updating, also with reference to the different categories of users;
f) the obligation to adopt the service charter on the basis of the current guidance acts;
g) the obligation to provide for the realization of the Program of interventions;
h) the methods of control of the correct exercise of the service and the obligation to prepare a technical system suitable for this purpose, as provided for in Article 165;
i) the duty to provide every collaboration for the organization and activation of the integrated control systems that the Area Authority has the faculty to arrange throughout the period of entrustment;
l) the obligation to give timely communication to the Area Authority of the occurrence of events that involve or make one foresee irregularities in the provision of the service, as well as the obligation to take every initiative for the elimination of the irregularities, in accordance with the prescriptions of the Area Authority itself;
m) the obligation of restitution, at the expiry of the entrustment, of the works, plants and channels of the integrated water service in conditions of efficiency and in a good state of conservation;
n) the obligation to provide suitable financial and insurance guarantees;
o) the penalties, the sanctions in case of non-fulfillment and the conditions of resolution according to the principles of the civil code;
p) the methods of reporting on the activities of the manager.
3. On the basis of the convention of paragraph 2, the Area Authority prepares a draft convention with its related specification, to be attached to the tender documents. Where the region or the autonomous province has not provided for the adoption of the standard conventions and specifications of paragraph 2, the Area Authority prepares the draft on the basis of the current legislation. Existing conventions must be integrated in accordance with the provisions of paragraph 2.
4. In the Specification attached to the Management Convention, the works and extraordinary maintenance, as well as the temporal and financial program of execution, must also be defined, on the basis of the program of interventions.
5. The entrustment of the service is subordinated to the provision by the manager of a suitable surety guarantee. This guarantee must cover the interventions to be carried out in the first five years of management and must be updated annually so as to cover the interventions to be carried out in the subsequent five-year period.
6. The manager shall update the Survey act within the terms established by the convention.
7. The concessionaire of the integrated water service, with the prior consent of the Area Authority, may manage other public services, in addition to the water service, but compatible with it, even if not extended to the entire optimal territorial area.
8. The concessionary companies of the integrated water service, as well as the mixed companies established following the identification of the private partner through a European tender, concessionaires of the service itself, may issue bonds subscribable exclusively by users with the faculty of conversion into ordinary or savings shares. In the case of an increase in the share capital, a quota of not less than ten percent is offered for subscription to the users of the service.

**Art. 152**
**Control and substitute powers**
1. The Area Authority has the faculty of access and verification to the water infrastructures, including during the construction phase.
2. In the case of non-fulfillment by the manager of the obligations deriving from the law or the convention, which compromise the resource or the environment or which do not allow the achievement of the minimum service levels, the Area Authority shall intervene promptly to guarantee the fulfillment by the manager, exercising all the powers conferred on it by the provisions of the law and the convention. If the non-fulfillment of the manager persists, and without prejudice to the consequent penalties at his expense, as well as the power of resolution and revocation, the Area Authority, after a warning, may replace him by having the works carried out by third parties, in respect of the current provisions on public procurement.
3. If the Area Authority does not intervene, or in any case delays its intervention, the region, after a warning and having heard the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), shall exercise the necessary substitute powers, by appointing an "ad acta" commissioner. If the region does not comply within forty-five days, the aforesaid substitute powers are exercised, after a warning to comply within the term of twenty days, by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, by appointing an "ad acta" commissioner.
4. The Area Authority shall communicate annually to the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) the results of the management controls.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 153**
**Assets of the managers of the integrated water service**
1. The water infrastructures owned by the local authorities pursuant to Article 143 are entrusted in free use concession, for the entire duration of the management, to the manager of the integrated water service, who assumes the relative charges in the terms provided for by the convention and its related specification.
2. The fixed assets, assets, and liabilities relating to the integrated water service, including the charges connected with the amortization of loans or the loans themselves, net of any non-repayable capital and/or interest grants, are transferred to the manager, who succeeds in the relative obligations. This transfer is taken into account in determining the tariff, in order to guarantee the invariance of the charges for public finance.

**Art. 154**
**Tariff of the integrated water service**
1. The tariff constitutes the consideration for the integrated water service and is determined taking into account the quality of the water resource and the service provided, the necessary works and adjustments, the extent of the costs of management of the works, the adequacy of the remuneration of the invested capital and the costs of management of the safeguard areas, as well as a share of the operating costs of the Area Authority, so as to ensure the full coverage of the investment and operating costs according to the principle of cost recovery and according to the "polluter pays" principle. All the components of the tariff of the integrated water service have the nature of consideration.
2. The Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, on the proposal of the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), taking into account the need to recover environmental costs also according to the "polluter pays" principle, defines by decree the cost components for the determination of the tariff relating to water services for the various sectors of water use.
3. In order to ensure a homogeneous discipline on the national territory, by decree of the Minister of Economy and Finance, in concert with the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, the general criteria for the determination, by the regions, of the concession fees for the use of public water are established, taking into account the environmental costs and the resource costs and also providing for reductions of the fee in the case in which the concessionaire implements a reuse of water by re-employing the water resulting downstream of the production process or a part of it or, again, returns the discharge water with the same qualitative characteristics as that withdrawn. The updating of the fees is triennial.
4. The Area Authority, for the purpose of preparing the Financial Plan referred to in Article 149, paragraph 1, letter c), determines the basic tariff, in compliance with the provisions contained in the decree referred to in paragraph 2, communicating it to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and to the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea.
5. The tariff is applied by the managers, in respect of the Convention and its related specification.
6. In the modulation of the tariff, facilities are ensured, including through compensations for other types of consumption, for essential domestic ones, as well as for the consumption of certain categories, according to pre-established income brackets. To achieve objectives of equitable redistribution of costs, tariff increases are permitted for second homes, for seasonal accommodation facilities, as well as for craft, commercial and industrial businesses.
7. The eventual modulation of the tariff among the municipalities takes into account the per capita investments for residents made by the municipalities themselves that are useful for the purposes of organizing the integrated water service.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."

**Art. 155**
**Tariff of the sewerage and purification service**
1. The tariff components referring to the public sewerage and purification services are due by the users even in the case where there are no purification plants or these are temporarily inactive. The manager is required to pay the relative proceeds, resulting from the tariff formulation defined pursuant to Article 154, into a restricted fund in the name of the Area Authority, which makes it available to the manager for the implementation of the interventions relating to the sewerage networks and purification plants provided for in the area plan. The tariff is not due if the user is equipped with their own collection and purification systems, provided that such systems have received specific approval from the Area Authority.
2. Pending the entrustment of the management of the local water services to the manager of the integrated water service, the municipalities already equipped with functioning purification plants, which are not in a state of financial distress, shall allocate the proceeds deriving from the purification and sewerage fee primarily to the maintenance of the plants themselves.
3. The users required to pay the tariff referring to the public sewerage service, referred to in paragraph 1, are exempt from the payment of any other tariff possibly due for the same title to other public bodies.
4. For the purpose of determining the tariff component referred to in this article, the volume of discharged water is determined as one hundred percent of the volume of water supplied.
5. For industrial users, the tariff component referred to in this article is determined on the basis of the quality and quantity of the discharged wastewater and on the basis of the "polluter pays" principle. The possibility of determining a reduced tariff component for users who provide directly for purification and who use the public sewer system is without prejudice, provided that their respective purification systems have received specific approval from the Area Authority.
6. For the purpose of encouraging the reuse of wastewater or already used water in the production cycle, the tariff for industrial users is reduced in function of the use in the production process of wastewater or already used water. The reduction is determined by applying a corrective factor to the tariff, which takes into account the quantity of reused water and the quantity of primary water used.

**Art. 156**
**Collection of the tariff**
1. The tariff is collected by the manager of the integrated water service. If the water service is managed separately, as a result of particular conventions and concessions, the relative tariff is collected by the manager of the aqueduct service, who provides for the subsequent distribution among the various interested managers within thirty days of collection.
2. With a specific convention, subject to the control of the region, the relations between the various managers for the distribution of the collection expenses are defined.
3. The voluntary and coercive collection of the tariff can be carried out according to the provisions of the decree of the President of the Republic No. 602 of 29 September 1973, by means of a convention with the Revenue Agency.

**Art. 157**
**Works for the adaptation of the water service**
1. The local authorities have the faculty to carry out the necessary works to provide for the adaptation of the water service in relation to urban plans and to concessions for new buildings in already urbanized areas, after an opinion of compatibility with the area plan rendered by the Area Authority and following a convention with the manager of the service itself, to whom the works, once realized, are entrusted in concession.

**Art. 158**
**Works and interventions for the transfer of water**
1. In order to plan the use of water resources, where the need involves or may involve the transfer of water between different regions and this goes beyond the reference areas of the hydrographic districts, the Basin Authorities, having heard the interested regions, shall promote program agreements between the regions themselves, pursuant to Article 34 of Legislative Decree No. 267 of 18 August 2000, in any case safeguarding the purposes of Article 144 of this decree. To this end, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and the Minister of Infrastructure and Transport, each for their own competence, shall jointly take the appropriate initiatives also at the request of a Basin Authority or an interested region or also in the presence of a request presented by other public subjects or by interested private subjects, setting a deadline for defining the agreements.
2. In case of inertia, of lack of agreement regarding the use of water resources, or of non-implementation of the agreement itself, the President of the Council of Ministers shall provide in a substitute capacity, after a warning to comply within a suitable term, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea.
3. The works and plants necessary for the purposes of this article are declared of national interest. Their realization and management, if of public initiative, can also be placed entirely at the expense of the State through quantification of the charge and its relative financial coverage, after deliberation of the Interministerial Committee for Economic Planning (CIPE), on the proposal of the Ministers of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and of Infrastructure and Transport, each for their respective competence. The Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall carry out the procedures for the concession of use of the water to the user subjects and defines the relative standard convention; the Minister of Infrastructure and Transport is responsible for determining the criteria and methods for the execution and management of the interventions, as well as the entrustment for the realization and management of the plants.

**TITLE III - SUPERVISION, CONTROLS AND PARTICIPATION**

**Art. 159** *[Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste]*
*[Repealed]*

**Art. 160** *[Tasks and functions of the Supervisory Authority]*
*[Repealed]*

**Art. 161**
**Observatory on water resources and waste**
1. The Authority, for the performance of its tasks, shall avail itself of an Observatory on the sectors of its competence. The Observatory carries out functions of collection, processing and restitution of statistical and cognitive data, forming a database connected with the information systems of the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, of the regions and of the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, of the Basin Authorities and of the public subjects who hold information in the sector. In particular, the Observatory collects and processes data concerning:
a) the census of the participants in the tenders for the entrustment of the services, as well as of the managing subjects in relation to the dimensional, technical and financial data of operation;
b) the general conditions of contract and conventions for the exercise of the services;
c) the models adopted of organization, management, control and programming of the services and plants;
d) the levels of quality of the services provided;
e) the tariffs applied;
f) the investment plans for the modernization of the plants and the development of the services.
2. The managers of the water services and of the collection and disposal of waste shall transmit every twelve months to the Observatory the data and information of paragraph 1 and in any case all the data that the Observatory requests from them at any time.
3. On the basis of the data acquired, the Observatory carries out, at the request of the Authority, processing for the purpose, among other things, of:
a) defining productivity indices for the evaluation of the economy of the managements against the services rendered;
b) identifying technological levels and optimal organizational models of the services;
c) defining evaluation parameters for the control of the tariff policies practiced, also in support of the decision-making bodies in the matter of setting tariffs and their constraints and adjustments, verifying compliance with the criteria set on the matter by the competent state bodies;
d) identifying situations of criticality and functional irregularity of the services or of non-observance of the current regulatory prescriptions on the matter;
e) promoting the experimentation and adoption of innovative technologies;
f) verifying the feasibility and congruity of the investment programs in relation to the financial resources and the tariff policy;
g) realizing summary cognitive frameworks.
4. The Observatory ensures generalized access, including by computer, to the data collected and to the processing carried out according to the deliberation of the Authority and in respect of the general provisions.
5. By decree of the President of the Council of Ministers, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Economy and Finance and with the Minister for Public Function, the organic structure of the Observatory, which is headed by a director, and the operating expenses are determined, in respect of the principle of the invariance of the charges borne by public finance. For the performance of its tasks, the Observatory, on the indication of the Authority, may avail itself of the consultancy of experts in the sector and stipulate conventions with public research bodies and with specialized companies.

**Art. 162**
**Participation, guarantee and information of users**
1. The manager of the integrated water service ensures information to users, promotes initiatives for the dissemination of the culture of water and guarantees the access of citizens to information concerning the services managed in the optimal territorial area of its competence, the technologies used, the functioning of the plants, the quantity and quality of the water supplied and treated.
2. The Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, the regions and the autonomous provinces, within their respective competencies, shall ensure the publicity of the projects concerning hydraulic works that involve or presuppose large and small derivations, damming or canalization works, as well as the drilling of wells. To this end, the competent administrations shall ensure the publication of the concession applications, concurrently with the start of the procedure, in addition to the forms provided for by Article 7 of the single text of the legal provisions on water and electrical plants, approved with Royal Decree No. 1775 of 11 December 1933, in at least one national daily newspaper and one local daily newspaper for large derivations of water from transnational and border rivers.
3. Anyone can view at the competent offices of the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, of the regions and of the autonomous provinces all the documents, acts, studies and projects relating to the concession applications referred to in paragraph 2 of this article, pursuant to the current provisions on the publicity of the acts of the public administrations.

**Art. 163**
**Management of safeguard areas**
1. To ensure the protection of the safeguard areas of water resources intended for human consumption, the manager of the integrated water service may stipulate conventions with the State, the regions, the local authorities, the associations and the agrarian universities holders of collective domains, for the direct management of the public or collective domains falling within the perimeter of the aforesaid areas, in respect of the protection of nature and taking into account the rights of civic use exercised.
2. The tariff component referred to the costs for the management of the safeguard areas, in case of transfers of water from one optimal territorial area to another, is paid to the mountain community, where established, or to the local authorities in whose territory the derivations fall; the relative proceeds are used for the purposes of the protection and recovery of environmental resources.

**Art. 164**
**Discipline of water in protected areas**
1. Within the national and regional protected natural areas, the managing body of the protected area, having heard the Basin Authority, defines the spring, flowing and groundwater necessary for the conservation of the ecosystems, which cannot be captured.
2. The recognition and preferential concession of the surface or spring waters that have assumed a public nature by effect of Article 1 of Law No. 36 of 5 January 1994, as well as the concessions in regularization, are issued upon the opinion of the managing body of the natural protected area. The managing bodies of protected areas verify the captures and derivations already granted within the areas themselves and request the competent authority to modify the quantities of release if they recognize alterations of the biological balances of the watercourses object of capture, without this giving rise to the payment of indemnities by the public administration, without prejudice to the relative reduction of the state concession fee.

**Art. 165**
**Controls**
1. To ensure the supply of good quality water and for the control of discharges into the receiving bodies, each manager of the water service shall equip itself with an adequate territorial control service and an analysis laboratory for the quality controls of the water at the intake, in the adduction and distribution networks, in the purifiers and in the treatment plants, or stipulates a specific convention with other managers of water services. The administrative competencies and the control functions on the quality of the water and on the discharges into the water bodies established by the current legislation and those of the technical bodies responsible for such functions remain firm.
2. Those who supply themselves in whole or in part with water from sources other than the public aqueduct are required to report annually to the manager of the water service the quantity withdrawn in the terms and according to the methods provided for by the legislation for the protection of water from pollution.
3. The sanctions provided for by Article 19 of Legislative Decree No. 31 of 2 February 2001, apply to the person responsible for the management of the aqueduct only in the case in which, after the communication of the outcome of the analyses, he has not promptly adopted the measures suitable to adapt the quality of the water or to prevent the consumption or supply of non-compliant water.

**TITLE IV - PRODUCTIVE USES OF WATER RESOURCES**

**Art. 166**
**Uses of irrigation and land reclamation waters**
1. The land reclamation and irrigation consortia, within their competencies, have the faculty to realize and manage the networks for predominantly irrigation purposes, the plants for the use in agriculture of wastewater, the rural aqueducts and the other plants functional to the irrigation and land reclamation systems and, upon application to the competent authorities accompanied by the project of the works to be realized, have the faculty to use the flowing waters in the consortial channels and ditches for uses that involve the restitution of the water and are compatible with the subsequent uses, including the production of hydroelectric energy and the supply of productive enterprises. The Basin Authority expresses its determination within one hundred and twenty days. After this term, the application is considered accepted. For such uses, the consortia are obliged to pay the relative fees for the corresponding quantities of water, with the provisions of the second paragraph of Article 36 of the single text of the legal provisions on water and electrical plants, approved with Royal Decree No. 1775 of 11 December 1933, also applying in such cases.
2. The relations between the land reclamation and irrigation consortia and the subjects who practice the uses of paragraph 1 are regulated by the provisions of chapter I of title VI of Royal Decree No. 368 of 8 May 1904.
3. Without prejudice to compliance with the discipline on the quality of water and discharges established by the third part of this decree, anyone who, not associated with the land reclamation and irrigation consortia, uses consortial channels or irrigation water as a receiver of discharges, even if purified and compatible with irrigation use, coming from settlements of any nature, must contribute to the expenses incurred by the consortium, taking into account the flow rate of discharged water.
4. The contribution of paragraph 3 is determined by the interested consortium and communicated to the user subject, together with the methods of payment.

**Art. 167**
**Agricultural uses of water**
1. In periods of drought and in any case in cases of scarcity of water resources, during which the regulation of the derivations in progress is carried out, the priority of agricultural use, including the aquaculture activity of Law No. 102 of 5 February 1992, must be ensured after human consumption.
2. In the case in which, pursuant to Article 145, paragraph 3, the regulation of the derivations is carried out, the competent administration, having heard the subjects holding the derivation concessions, shall take the relative measures.
3. The collection of rainwater in reservoirs and tanks serving agricultural lands or single buildings is free.
4. The collection referred to in paragraph 3 does not require a license or concession for the derivation of water; the realization of the relative structures is regulated by the laws on construction, on constructions in seismic zones, on dams and weirs and by other special laws.
1. The use of groundwater for domestic uses, as defined by Article 93, second paragraph, of the single text of the legal provisions on water and electrical plants, approved with Royal Decree No. 1775 of 11 December 1933, remains regulated by the same provision, provided it does not compromise the equilibrium of the water balance of Article 145 of this decree.

**Art. 168**
**Use of water intended for hydroelectric use**
1. Taking into account the principles of the third part of this decree and of the national energy plan, as well as the guidelines for the multiple uses of water resources, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, having heard the Basin Authorities, as well as the regions and autonomous provinces, shall regulate, without this giving rise to the payment of indemnities by the public administration, without prejudice to the corresponding reduction of the concession fee:
a) the production for the purpose of the sale of desalinated water obtained in the production cycles of coastal power plants;
b) the use of impounded water for hydroelectric purposes to face situations of water emergency;
c) the defense and remediation for the safeguarding of the quantity and quality of the water of the reservoirs for hydroelectric use.

**Art. 169**
**Plans, studies and research**
1. The plans, studies and research carried out by the State Administrations and by public bodies with competence in the matters regulated by the third part of this decree are communicated to the competent Basin Authorities for the territory for the purposes of the preparation of the plans entrusted to them.

**SECTION IV - TRANSITIONAL AND FINAL PROVISIONS**

**Art. 170**
**Transitional norms**
1. For the purposes of the application of Article 65, limited to the procedures for the adoption and approval of the basin plans, until the date of entry into force of the second part of this decree, the procedures for the adoption and approval of the basin plans provided for by Law No. 183 of 18 May 1989 continue to apply.
2. For the purposes of the application of Article 1 of decree-law no. 279 of 12 October 2000, converted, with modifications, by law no. 365 of 11 December 2000, the references contained therein to Article 1 of decree-law no. 180 of 11 June 1998, converted, with modifications, by law no. 267 of 3 August 1998, must be understood as referring to Article 66 of this decree; i references to Law no. 183 of 18 May 1989, are to be understood as referring to the first section of the third part of this decree, where compatible.
2-bis. Pending the establishment of the hydrographic districts referred to in Title II of the Third Part of this decree and the revision of the related legislative discipline with a corrective legislative decree, the basin authorities under Law no. 183 of 18 May 1989, are extended until the date of entry into force of the corrective decree which, pursuant to article 1, paragraph 6, of Law no. 308 of 2004, defines the related discipline.*
3. For the purposes of applying the third part of this decree:
a) until the issuance of the decrees referred to in article 95, paragraphs 4 and 5, the ministerial decree of 28 July 2004 continues to apply;
b) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 99, paragraph 1, the ministerial decree no. 185 of 12 June 2003 continues to apply;
c) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 104, paragraph 4, the ministerial decree of 28 July 1994 applies;
d) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 112, paragraph 2, the ministerial decree of 6 July 2005 applies;
e) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 114, paragraph 4, the ministerial decree of 30 June 2004 continues to apply;
f) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 118, paragraph 2, the ministerial decree of 18 September 2002 and the ministerial decree of 19 August 2003 continue to apply;
g) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 123, paragraph 2, the ministerial decree of 19 August 2003 continues to apply;
h) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 146, paragraph 3, the ministerial decree no. 99 of 8 January 1997 continues to apply;
i) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 150, paragraph 2, the entrustment of the concession for the management of the integrated water service as well as the entrustment to mixed companies, the ministerial decree of 22 November 2001, as well as the circulars of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea of 6 December 2004, continue to apply;
l) until the issuance of the decree referred to in article 154, paragraph 2, the ministerial decree of 1 August 1996 continues to apply.
4. The third part of this decree contains the rules for transposing the following Community directives:
a) Directive 75/440/EEC on the quality of surface water intended for the production of drinking water;
b) Directive 76/464/EEC on pollution caused by certain dangerous substances discharged into the aquatic environment;
c) Directive 78/659/EEC on the quality of fresh waters needing protection or improvement in order to support fish life;
d) Directive 79/869/EEC concerning the methods of measurement and frequencies of sampling and analysis of surface water intended for the production of drinking water;
e) Directive 79/923/EEC on the quality required of shellfish waters;
f) Directive 80/68/EEC on the protection of groundwater against pollution caused by certain dangerous substances;
g) Directive 82/176/EEC on limit values and quality objectives for mercury discharges by the chlor-alkali electrolysis industry;
h) Directive 83/513/EEC on limit values and quality objectives for cadmium discharges;
i) Directive 84/156/EEC on limit values and quality objectives for mercury discharges by sectors other than the chlor-alkali electrolysis industry;
l) Directive 84/491/EEC on limit values and quality objectives for discharges of hexachlorocyclohexane;
m) Directive 88/347/EEC amending Annex 11 to Directive 86/280/EEC concerning the limit values and quality objectives for discharges of certain dangerous substances included in list 1 of the Annex to Directive 76/464/EEC;
n) Directive 90/415/EEC amending Directive 86/280/EEC concerning the limit values and quality objectives for discharges of certain dangerous substances included in list 1 of Directive 76/464/EEC;
o) Directive 91/271/EEC concerning urban waste-water treatment;
p) Directive 91/676/EEC concerning the protection of waters against pollution caused by nitrates from agricultural sources;
q) Directive 98/15/EC amending Directive 91/271/EEC with regard to certain requirements of Annex 1;
r) Directive 2000/60/EC, establishing a framework for Community action in the field of water policy.
5. The regions shall define, in terms of no less than two years, the timeframes for adaptation to the prescriptions, including those adopted pursuant to article 101, paragraph 2, contained in the regional legislation implementing the third part of this decree and in the protection plans referred to in article 121.
6. The provisions of art. 36 of Law no. 128 of 24 April 1998, and of the legislative decrees implementing Directive 96/92/EC remain unaffected.
7. Until the issuance of the regional discipline referred to in article 112, the activities of agronomic utilization shall be carried out according to the regional provisions in force at the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree.
8. The implementation of the third part of this decree shall not result in new or increased charges or reduced revenues for public finance.
9. A share of not less than ten percent and not more than fifteen percent of the allocations provided for by state financing provisions is reserved for monitoring and study activities aimed at the implementation of the third part of this decree.
10. The provisions regarding the defense of the sea remain unaffected.
11. Until the issuance of corresponding acts adopted in implementation of the third part of this decree, the provisions and acts issued in implementation of the laws repealed by article 175 remain valid and effective.
12. The burden deriving from the establishment and functioning of the Section for the supervision of water resources is covered by using the resources referred to in art. 22, paragraph 6, of Law no. 36 of 5 January 1994.
13. The burden deriving from the establishment and functioning of the Section for the supervision of waste, equal to one million two hundred and forty thousand euros, updated annually in relation to the inflation rate, is covered by the National Packaging Consortium referred to in article 224 with a contribution of an equal amount charged to the consortia members. Said sums are paid by the National Packaging Consortium to the State budget entry to be reallocated by decree of the Minister of Economy and Finance to a specific chapter of the budget forecast of the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea.
14. In the first application, the term of one hundred and eighty days referred to in article 112, paragraph 2, shall run from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree.
NOTE: "paragraph 2-bis" was inserted by Legislative Decree no. 284/2006 of 8 November (G.U. no. 274 of 24/11/2006). Art. 1 paragraph 4 of Legislative Decree no. 284 of 8 November 2006 thus provides: "Until the date of entry into force of the corrective legislative decree referred to in paragraph 2-bis of article 170 of legislative decree no. 152 of 3 April 2006, as inserted by paragraph 3, the acts put in place by the basin authorities from 30 April 2006 are saved"

Art. 171
Fees for the use of public water
Pending the transfer of the water domain to the Sicily region, for large derivations undergoing regularization pursuant to article 96, paragraph 6, located in the territory of that region, the following annual fees shall apply retroactively, starting from 1 January 2002:
a) for each module of water granted for irrigation use, 40.00 euros, reduced by half if the seepage and residual water are returned, including to the aquifer;
b) for each hectare of the irrigated district granted, with a derivation not subject to fixed-rate measurement, 0.40 euros;
c) for each module of water granted for human consumption, 1,750.00 euros, minimum 300.00 euros;
d) for each module of water granted for industrial use, 12,600.00 euros, minimum 1,750.00 euros. The fee is reduced by fifty percent if the concessionaire implements a reuse of water by re-employing the water resulting downstream of the production process or a part of it, or, again, if it returns the discharge water with the same qualitative characteristics as that withdrawn. The provisions of paragraph 5 of article 12 of decree-law no. 90 of 27 April 1990, converted, with modifications, by law no. 1651 of 26 June 1990, do not apply for industrial use;
e) for each module of water granted for fish farming, irrigation of sports facilities and public green areas, 300.00 euros, minimum 100.00 euros;
f) for each kilowatt of nominal power granted, for hydroelectric use derivation concessions, 12.00 euros, minimum 100.00 euros;
g) for each module of water granted for hygienic and similar use, concerning the use of water for hygienic and fire-fighting services, including that related to sports facilities, industries, and various structures where the concession only concerns such use, for car washing and road washing facilities, and in any case for all uses not provided for in letters from a) to f), 900.00 euros.
The amounts of the fees referred to in paragraph 1 may not be less than 250.00 euros for derivations for human consumption and 1,500.00 euros for derivations for industrial use.
Art. 172
Existing management
The Area Authorities that, at the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, have already proceeded with the drafting of the area plan, without having chosen the form of management and started the entrustment procedures, are required, within the six months following that date, to deliberate the aforementioned provisions.
In relation to the expiry of the term referred to in paragraph 15-bis of article 113 of legislative decree no. 267 of 18 August 2000, the Area Authority shall arrange for the new entrustments, in compliance with the third part of this decree, within the sixty days preceding that expiry.
If the Area Authority does not proceed with the fulfillments referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2 within the terms established therein, the region, within thirty days, shall exercise, giving communication to the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea and to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), the substitute powers, appointing an "ad acta" commissioner, whose expenses are charged to the defaulting entity, who starts the entrustment procedures within thirty days, determining the deadlines for the individual procedural fulfillments. If the regional commissioner does not proceed within the terms so established, the substitute powers aimed at completing the entrustment procedure fall to the President of the Council of Ministers, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea.
If the local authorities do not join the Area Authorities pursuant to article 148 within sixty days from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, the region shall exercise, after warning the local authority to comply within the term of thirty days and giving communication to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*), the substitute powers, appointing an "ad acta" commissioner, whose expenses are charged to the defaulting entity.
Upon expiry, or early termination, of the managements in place pursuant to paragraph 2, the assets and plants of the already concessionaire companies are transferred directly to the granting local authority within the limits and according to the methods provided for in the convention.
The aqueduct, sewerage, and purification plants managed by the consortia for the industrial areas and nuclei referred to in article 50 of the single text of the laws on interventions in Southern Italy, approved by decree of the President of the Republic no. 218 of 6 March 1978, by other consortia or public bodies, in compliance with the management unit, are transferred by 31 December 2006 in use concession to the manager of the integrated water service of the Optimal Territorial Area in which all or the majority of the served territories fall, according to a plan adopted by decree of the President of the Council of Ministers, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, having heard the regions, the provinces, and the interested entities.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."
Art. 173
Personnel
Without prejudice to the regional legislation adopted pursuant to art. 12, paragraph 3, of Law no. 36 of 5 January 1994, the personnel who, as of 31 December 2005 or in any case eight months before the entrustment of the service, belong to the municipal administrations, to the former municipal or consortium companies and to private companies, including cooperatives, that operate in the water services sector shall be subject, without prejudice to the termination of the employment relationship, to direct and immediate transfer to the new manager of the integrated water service, with the safeguarding of the contractual, collective and individual conditions in place. In the case of transfer of employees of public entities and former municipal or consortium companies and of private companies, including cooperatives, to the manager of the integrated water service, the discipline of the transfer of a business branch referred to in art. 2112 of the civil code applies, pursuant to article 31 of Legislative Decree no. 165 of 30 March 2001.
Art. 174
Implementation and execution provisions
Until the adoption by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea of new implementing provisions of the third section of the third part of this decree, the decree of the President of the Council of Ministers of 4 March 1996, published in the Official Gazette no. 62 of 14 March 1994, applies.
The Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, having heard the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste(*) and the permanent Conference for relations between the State, the regions, and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, within one year from the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, within the framework of specific institutional agreements, shall prepare a specific program for the achievement, without additional charges for the Ministry, of the purification levels, as defined by directive 91/271/EEC, activating the substitute powers of article 152 in the optimal territorial areas where there are agglomerations for which infringement procedures are pending for violation of the cited directive.
(*) Note: the text of art. 1, c. 5 of D.Lgs. 284/2006 is reported below:
"5. Articles 159, 160, and 207 of Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are repealed and the Committee for the supervision of the use of water resources and the National Observatory on waste are reconstituted and exercise their respective functions. All references to the Supervisory Authority on water resources and waste contained in Legislative Decree No. 152 of April 3, 2006, are suppressed."
Art. 175
Repeal of norms
From the date of entry into force of the third part of this decree, the norms contrary to or incompatible with it are or remain repealed, and in particular:
a) art. 42, third paragraph, of Royal Decree no. 1775 of 11 December 1933, as amended by article 8 of Legislative Decree no. 275 of 12 July 1993;
b) Law no. 319 of 10 May 1976;
c) Law no. 690 of 8 October 1976, converting, with modifications, decree-law no. 544 of 10 August 1976;
d) Law no. 650 of 24 December 1979;
e) Law no. 62 of 5 March 1982, converting, with modifications, decree-law no. 801 of 30 December 1981;
f) decree of the President of the Republic no. 515 of 3 July 1982;
g) Law no. 381 of 25 July 1984, converting, with modifications, decree-law no. 176 of 29 May 1984;
h) articles 5, 6, and 7 of Law no. 7 of 24 January 1986, converting, with modifications, decree-law no. 667 of 25 November 1985;
i) articles 4, 5, 6, and 7 of the decree of the President of the Republic no. 236 of 24 May 1988;
l) Law no. 183 of 18 May 1989;
m) articles 4 and 5 of Law no. 71 of 5 April 1990, converting, with modifications, decree-law no. 16 of 5 February 1990;
n) art. 32 of Law no. 9 of 9 January 1991;
o) Legislative Decree no. 130 of 25 January 1992;

Art. 176
Final norm
The provisions of the third part of this decree that concern matters of concurrent legislation constitute fundamental principles pursuant to article 117, paragraph 3, of the Constitution.
The provisions of the third part of this decree are applicable in the special statute regions and in the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano compatibly with the norms of their respective statutes.
For the waters belonging to the water domain of the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, the competencies regarding the use of public waters and regarding hydraulic works provided for by the special statute of the Trentino-Alto Adige region and by the relative implementation norms remain unaffected.
PART FOUR - NORMS ON WASTE MANAGEMENT AND REMEDIATION OF CONTAMINATED SITES
Note: Paragraph 184 of art. 1 of the 2007 Finance Act is reported below:
"184. Pending the full implementation of the provisions laid down by Legislative Decree no. 152 of 3 April 2006, and subsequent amendments:
a) the levy regime relating to the waste collection and disposal service adopted in each municipality for the year 2006 shall remain unchanged also for the year 2007;
b) regarding the assimilation of special waste to urban waste, the provisions of articles 18, paragraph 2, letter d), and 57, paragraph 1, of Legislative Decree no. 22 of 5 February 1997 (...) continue to apply"
TITLE I - WASTE MANAGEMENT
CHAPTER I - GENERAL PROVISIONS
Art. 177
Scope of application
The fourth part of this decree regulates waste management and the remediation of contaminated sites, also in implementation of the community directives on waste, on hazardous waste, on used oils, on spent batteries, on packaging waste, on polychlorinated biphenyls (PCBs), on landfills, on incinerators, on electrical and electronic waste, on port waste, on end-of-life vehicles, on sanitary waste and on waste containing asbestos. Specific, particular, or complementary provisions, conforming to the principles of the fourth part of this decree, adopted in implementation of community directives that regulate the management of certain categories of waste, are unaffected.
The regions and autonomous provinces shall adapt their respective legal systems to the provisions on environmental and ecosystem protection contained in the fourth part of this decree within one year from the date of its entry into force.
Art. 178
Purpose
Waste management constitutes an activity of public interest and is regulated by the fourth part of this decree in order to ensure a high level of environmental protection and effective controls, taking into account the specificity of hazardous waste.
Waste must be recovered or disposed of without danger to human health and without using processes or methods that could harm the environment, and, in particular:
a) without creating risks for water, air, soil, as well as for fauna and flora;
b) without causing nuisance from noise or odors;
c) without damaging the landscape and sites of particular interest, protected on the basis of current legislation.
Waste management is carried out in accordance with the principles of precaution, prevention, proportionality, responsibility, and cooperation of all subjects involved in the production, distribution, use, and consumption of goods from which waste originates, in compliance with the principles of the national and community legal system, with particular reference to the community principle "polluter pays". To this end, waste management is carried out according to criteria of effectiveness, efficiency, economy, and transparency.
To achieve the purposes and objectives of the fourth part of this decree, the State, the regions, the autonomous provinces, and the local authorities shall exercise the powers and functions of their respective competence in waste management in accordance with the provisions of the fourth part of this decree, adopting every appropriate action and availing themselves, where appropriate, through agreements, program contracts or experimental memoranda of understanding, of public or private subjects.
The subjects referred to in paragraph 4 also constitute a complete and synergistic system that harmonizes, in a unitary context, relatively to the objectives to be pursued, the drafting of technical standards, accreditation systems, and certification systems relating directly or indirectly to environmental matters, with particular reference to waste management, according to the criteria and with the methods of article 195, paragraph 2, letter a), and in compliance with the information procedures in the sector of technical standards and regulations and of the rules relating to the services of the information society, provided for by the community directives and related implementation norms, with particular reference to Law no. 317 of 21 June 1986.

Art. 179
Priority criteria in waste management
Public administrations shall pursue, in the exercise of their respective competencies, initiatives aimed at giving priority to the prevention and reduction of the production and harmfulness of waste, in particular through:
a) the development of clean technologies that allow a more rational use and a greater saving of natural resources;
b) the technical development and placing on the market of products designed so as not to contribute or to contribute as little as possible, through their manufacture, use, or disposal, to increasing the quantity or harmfulness of waste and the risks of pollution;
c) the development of appropriate techniques for the elimination of hazardous substances contained in waste in order to facilitate its recovery.
In compliance with the priority measures referred to in paragraph 1, public administrations shall also adopt measures aimed at the recovery of waste through recycling, reuse, reutilization, or any other action intended to obtain secondary raw materials, as well as the use of waste as a source of energy.
Art. 180
Prevention of waste production
In order to promote as a priority the prevention and reduction of the production and harmfulness of waste, the initiatives of article 179 concern in particular:
a) the promotion of economic instruments, eco-balances, environmental certification systems, life cycle analysis of products, information and consumer awareness actions, the use of quality systems, as well as the development of the ecological label system for the correct evaluation of the impact of a specific product on the environment during the entire life cycle of the product itself;
b) the provision of tender clauses that enhance the technical capabilities and skills in waste production prevention;
c) the promotion of agreements and program contracts or experimental memoranda of understanding aimed at, with improving effects, the prevention and reduction of the quantity and hazardousness of waste;
d) the implementation of Legislative Decree no. 59 of 18 February 2005, and of the other decrees transposing Directive 96/61/EC on integrated pollution prevention and reduction.
Art. 181
Recovery of waste
For the purpose of proper waste management, public administrations shall favor the reduction of the final disposal of waste through:
a) reuse, re-employment, and recycling;
b) other forms of recovery to obtain secondary raw materials from waste;
c) the adoption of economic measures and the provision of contract conditions that prescribe the use of materials recovered from waste in order to favor the market for such materials;
d) the use of waste as a means to produce energy.
In order to favor and increase the activities of reuse, re-employment, and recycling and the adoption of other forms of recovery of waste, public administrations and producers shall promote analyses of the life cycles of products, eco-balances, information campaigns, and all other useful initiatives.
Companies that intend to modify their production cycles in order to reduce the quantity and hazardousness of the waste produced or to favor the recovery of materials are granted priority access to the benefits from the special revolving fund for technological innovation, provided for by articles 14 and following of Law no. 46 of 17 February 1982. The methods, times, and procedures for the granting and disbursement of the aforementioned benefits are established by decree of the Minister of Productive Activities, in concert with the Ministers of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, of Economy and Finance, and of Health.
Public administrations shall promote and stipulate program agreements and contracts with the interested economic subjects or with the category associations representing the interested sectors, in order to favor the reuse, re-employment, recycling, and other forms of recovery of waste, as well as the use of secondary raw materials, of fuels or products obtained from the recovery of waste from separate collection. In compliance with the principles and criteria provided for by community norms and national transposition norms, said agreements and program contracts shall implement the provisions of the fourth part of this decree, in addition to establishing simplifications in administrative fulfillments in compliance with community norms and with the eventual recourse to economic instruments.
The agreements and program contracts of paragraph 4 are published in the Official Gazette and are open to the accession of interested subjects, in accordance with the communication of the Commission to the European Parliament, the Council and the Committee of the Regions, Com (2002) 412 final of 17 July 2002, on the basis of which the Commission may also use them in the context of self-regulation, understood as encouragement or recognition of the agreements themselves, or co-regulation, understood as a proposal to the legislator to use the agreements, where appropriate.
The methods of recovery of waste used to obtain secondary raw materials, fuels or products must guarantee the obtaining of materials with characteristics established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, pursuant to art. 17, paragraph 3, of Law no. 400 of 23 August 1988. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the ministerial decree of 5 February 1998 and of the decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea no. 161 of 12 June 2002 continue to apply. The aforesaid characteristics may also comply with the authorizations issued pursuant to articles 208, 209, and 210 of this decree.
In compliance with the provisions of paragraphs 4, 5, and 6 of this article, the interested economic subjects or the category associations representing the interested sectors, including with reference to entire economic and productive sectors, may stipulate with the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities and after hearing the opinion of the Economic and Social Council for Environmental Policies (CESPA), specific program agreements pursuant to paragraph 4 and article 206 to define the methods of recovery of waste intended for obtaining secondary raw materials, fuels, or products. The agreements shall establish the administrative procedures and fulfillments for the collection, for the reservation, for the transport of waste, for their commercialization, including through the telematic market, with particular reference to that of the recovery realized by the Chambers of Commerce, and for the controls of the characteristics and the relative testing methods; the same agreements shall also establish the characteristics of the secondary raw materials, fuels or products obtained, as well as the methods to ensure in any case their traceability until entry into the plant of effective use.
The proposal for a program agreement, with indication also of the methods used for the transport and for the use of the secondary raw materials, or the request for adhesion to an agreement already in force must be submitted to the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, who avails himself for the investigation of the National Committee of the Register referred to in article 212 and of the Agency for the Protection of the Environment and for Technical Services (APAT), which avails itself of the Regional Agencies for the Protection of the Environment (ARPA). On the proposal for an agreement, the opinion of the Authority referred to in article 207 is also acquired.
The agreements referred to in paragraph 7 must also contain, for each type of activity, the general norms that establish the types and quantities of waste and the conditions under which the waste recovery activity is exempted from authorization, in compliance with the conditions set by article 178, paragraph 2.
The signatories of the agreements provided for in this article are registered in a special section to be established at the Register referred to in article 212, upon simple written request, and without being subject to the financial guarantees of paragraphs 7 and 9 of the cited article 212.
The program agreements referred to in paragraph 7 are approved, for the purpose of their effectiveness, by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities and with the Minister of Health, and are subsequently published in the Official Gazette. Such agreements are open to the accession of all interested subjects.
The discipline on waste management applies until the completion of the recovery operations, which is realized when no further treatments are necessary for the substances, materials, and objects obtained to be used in an industrial or commercial process or marketed as a secondary raw material, fuel, or as a product to be placed, provided that the holder does not dispose of it or has not decided, or has no obligation, to dispose of it.
The discipline on waste management does not apply to materials, substances or objects that, without the need for transformation operations, already have the characteristics of secondary raw materials, fuels or products identified pursuant to this article, unless the holder disposes of them or has decided, or has the obligation, to dispose of them.
The subjects who transport or use secondary raw materials, fuels or products, in compliance with the provisions of this article, are not subject to the legislation on waste, unless they dispose of them or have decided, or have the obligation, to dispose of them.
Art. 182
Waste disposal
The disposal of waste is carried out in safe conditions and constitutes the residual phase of waste management, after verification, by the competent authority, of the technical and economic impossibility of carrying out the recovery operations referred to in article 181. To this end, the aforesaid verification concerns the availability of technologies developed on a scale that allows their application in economically and technically valid conditions in the relevant industrial sector, taking into consideration the costs and benefits, regardless of whether they are applied or produced domestically, provided they can be accessed under reasonable conditions.
Waste to be sent for final disposal must be reduced as much as possible both in mass and in volume, enhancing prevention and reuse, recycling, and recovery activities.
The disposal of waste is carried out with recourse to an integrated and adequate network of disposal plants, through the best available techniques and taking into account the relationship between the costs and the overall benefits, in order to:
a) achieve self-sufficiency in the disposal of non-hazardous urban waste in optimal territorial areas;
b) allow the disposal of waste in one of the most appropriate plants closest to the places of production or collection, in order to reduce the movements of the waste itself, taking into account the geographical context or the need for specialized plants for certain types of waste;
c) use the most suitable methods and technologies to guarantee a high degree of protection for the environment and public health.
In compliance with the prescriptions contained in Legislative Decree no. 133 of 11 May 2005, the construction and management of new plants can be authorized only if the relative combustion process is accompanied by energy recovery with a minimum quota of transformation of the calorific value of the waste into useful energy, calculated on an annual basis, established with appropriate technical norms approved by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, taking into account any existing sector technical norms, including at the community level.
It is forbidden to dispose of non-hazardous urban waste in regions other than those where it is produced, without prejudice to any regional or international agreements, if the territorial aspects and the technical-economic opportunity of reaching optimal levels of user service require it. The fractions of urban waste subject to separate collection intended for recovery are excluded from the ban, for which free circulation on the national territory is always permitted in order to favor their recovery as much as possible, privileging the concept of proximity to the recovery plants.
The disposal of waste in the sewer system is regulated by article 107, paragraph 3.
The activities of waste disposal in landfills are regulated according to the provisions of Legislative Decree no. 36 of 13 January 2003, implementing Directive 1999/31/EC.
The disposal of the biodegradable fraction obtained from the physical separation treatment of the residual fraction of solid urban waste is permitted within the wastewater treatment plants after a technical check of the plants by the managing body.
Art. 183
Definitions
For the purposes of the fourth part of this decree and without prejudice to the further definitions contained in the special provisions, it is intended by:
