a) waste: any substance or object that falls into the categories listed in Annex A to the fourth part of this decree and of which the holder disposes or has decided or has the obligation to dispose;
b) producer: the person whose activity has produced waste, i.e., the initial producer, and the person who has carried out pretreatment, mixing, or other operations that have changed the nature or composition of said waste;
c) holder: the producer of the waste or the subject who holds it;
d) management: the collection, transport, recovery, and disposal of waste, including the control of these operations, as well as the control of landfills after closure;
e) collection: the operation of withdrawal, sorting, or grouping of waste for its transport;
f) separate collection: the collection suitable, according to criteria of economy, effectiveness, transparency, and efficiency, to group urban waste into homogeneous commodity fractions, at the time of collection or, for the wet organic fraction, also at the time of treatment, as well as to group packaging waste separately from other urban waste, provided that all the above-mentioned waste is effectively destined for recovery.
g) disposal: any operation aimed at permanently removing a substance, a material, or an object from the economic and/or collection circuit and, in particular, the operations provided for in Annex B to the fourth part of this decree;
h) recovery: the operations that use waste to generate secondary raw materials, fuels, or products, through mechanical, thermal, chemical, or biological treatments, including sorting or selection, and, in particular, the operations provided for in Annex C to the fourth part of this decree;
i) place of waste production: one or more buildings or establishments or infrastructural sites connected to each other within a delimited area in which the production activities from which the waste originated are carried out;
l) storage: the disposal activities consisting of the preliminary deposit operations of waste referred to in point D 15 of Annex B to the fourth part of this decree, as well as the recovery activities consisting of the reservation operations of materials referred to in point R13 of Annex C to the same fourth part;
m) temporary storage: the grouping of waste carried out, before collection, at the place where it is produced, under the following conditions:
the stored waste must not contain polychlorodibenzodioxins, polychlorodibenzofurans, polychlorodibenzophenols in quantities exceeding 2.5 parts per million (ppm), nor polychlorobiphenyls and polychlorotriphenyls in quantities exceeding 25 parts per million (ppm);
hazardous waste must be collected and sent for recovery or disposal operations according to the following alternative methods, at the producer's choice:
2.1) at least every two months, regardless of the quantities in storage; or
2.2) when the quantity of hazardous waste in storage reaches 10 cubic meters. In any case, when the quantity of waste does not exceed 10 cubic meters per year, the temporary storage cannot last more than one year; or
2.3) limited to temporary storage carried out in establishments located on the smaller islands, within the maximum duration of one year, regardless of the quantities;
non-hazardous waste must be collected and sent for recovery or disposal operations according to the following alternative methods, at the producer's choice:
3.1) at least every three months, regardless of the quantities in storage; or
3.2) when the quantity of non-hazardous waste in storage reaches 20 cubic meters. In any case, when the quantity of waste does not exceed 20 cubic meters per year, the temporary storage cannot last more than one year; or
3.3) limited to temporary storage carried out in establishments located on the smaller islands, within the maximum duration of one year, regardless of the quantities;
the temporary storage must be carried out for homogeneous categories of waste and in compliance with the relative technical norms, as well as, for hazardous waste, in compliance with the norms that regulate the storage of the hazardous substances contained therein;
the norms that regulate the packaging and labeling of hazardous waste must be respected;
n) by-product: the products of the company's activity which, although not constituting the object of the main activity, arise continuously from the industrial process of the company itself and are intended for a further use or consumption. The by-products of which the company does not dispose, is not obliged to dispose, and has not decided to dispose, and in particular the by-products used directly by the company that produces them or marketed under economically favorable conditions for the company itself directly for consumption or use, without the need to carry out preliminary transformations in a subsequent production process, are not subject to the provisions of the fourth part of this decree; for this purpose, for preliminary transformation is meant any operation that causes the by-product to lose its identity, i.e., the commodity quality characteristics and the properties it already possesses, and which is necessary for its subsequent use in a production process or for consumption. The use of the by-product must be certain and not eventual. Also included among the by-products not subject to the provisions of the fourth part of this decree are pyrite cinders, iron oxide powders, from the process of roasting the mineral known as pyrite or iron sulfide for the production of sulfuric acid and iron oxide, deposited at disused production plants, industrial and non-industrial areas, even if subjected to a remediation or environmental restoration procedure. In order to guarantee a certain use of the by-product, compliance with commodity standards, as well as with technical, safety, and sector norms must be verified and the destination of the by-product for effective use based on these standards and norms must be attested through a declaration of the producer or holder, countersigned by the owner of the plant where the effective use takes place. The use of the by-product must not entail worse conditions for the environment or health compared to those of normal production activities;
o) wet fraction: putrescible organic waste with a high moisture content, from separate collection or selection or treatment of urban waste;
p) dry fraction: waste with low putrescibility and low moisture content from separate collection or selection or treatment of urban waste, having a significant energy content;
q) secondary raw material: substance or material having the characteristics established pursuant to article 181;
r) refuse-derived fuel (RDF): the fuel classifiable, on the basis of the technical standards UNI 9903-1 and subsequent modifications and integrations, as normal quality RDF, which is recovered from urban and special non-hazardous waste through treatments aimed at guaranteeing a calorific value suitable for its use, as well as to reduce and control:
the environmental and health risk;
the presence of metallic material, glass, inert materials, putrescible material, and the moisture content;
the presence of hazardous substances, in particular for the purpose of combustion;
s) high-quality refuse-derived fuel (CDR-Q): the fuel classifiable, on the basis of the technical standards UNI 9903-1 and subsequent modifications and integrations, as high-quality RDF, to which article 229 applies;
t) compost from waste: product obtained from the composting of the organic fraction of urban waste in compliance with specific technical norms aimed at defining its contents and uses compatible with environmental and health protection and, in particular, at defining its quality grades;
u) secondary raw material for steel and metallurgical activities whose use is certain and not eventual:
ferrous and non-ferrous scrap resulting from complete recovery operations and meeting Ceca, Aisi, Caef, Uni, Euro or other national and international specifications, identified within one hundred and eighty days from the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, not having a regulatory nature;
scrap or waste from industrial or artisanal processing or from production or consumption cycles, excluding separate collection, which originally possess the same characteristics reported in the specifications of number 1). The suppliers and producers of secondary raw material for steel activities belonging to foreign countries shall apply for registration with the National Register of Environmental Managers, pursuant to article 212, paragraph 12, within sixty days from the date of entry into force of the ministerial decree of number 1);
v) manager of the waste management and site remediation service: the company that carries out the waste management service, also produced by third parties, and the remediation of contaminated sites by resorting to, and coordinating, other companies possessing the legal requirements for the performance of individual parts of the service itself. The company that intends to carry out the waste management and site remediation activity must be registered in the categories of waste intermediation and site remediation of the Register referred to in article 212 as well as in the category of general works of remediation and environmental protection established by Annex A attached to the regulation referred to in the decree of the President of the Republic no. 34 of 25 January 2000;
z) emissions: any solid, liquid, or gaseous substance introduced into the atmosphere that may cause atmospheric pollution;
aa) water discharges: any discharge of wastewater into surface waters, on the ground, in the subsoil, and in the sewer network, regardless of their polluting nature, even if subjected to prior purification treatment;
bb) atmospheric pollution: any atmospheric modification due to the introduction into the air of one or more substances in quantities and with characteristics such as to harm or constitute a danger to human health or to the quality of the environment or such as to harm material goods or compromise the legitimate uses of the environment;
cc) integrated waste management: the complex of activities aimed at optimizing waste management, including the activity of street sweeping, as defined in letter d);
dd) street sweeping: method of collecting waste on the street.

Art. 184
Classification
For the purposes of implementing the fourth part of this decree, waste is classified, according to its origin, into urban waste and special waste and, according to its hazardous characteristics, into hazardous waste and non-hazardous waste.
Urban waste is:
a) domestic waste, including bulky waste, from premises and places used for civil housing;
b) non-hazardous waste from premises and places used for uses other than those of letter a), assimilated to urban waste for quality and quantity, pursuant to article 198, paragraph 2, letter g);
c) waste from street sweeping;
d) waste of any nature or origin, lying on public roads and areas or on private roads and areas in any case subject to public use or on sea and lake beaches and on the banks of watercourses;
e) plant waste from green areas, such as gardens, parks, and cemetery areas;
f) waste from exhumations and disinterments, as well as other waste from cemetery activities other than those of letters b), c), and e).
Special waste is:
a) waste from agricultural and agro-industrial activities;
b) waste deriving from demolition, construction activities, as well as hazardous waste deriving from excavation activities, without prejudice to the provisions of article 186;
c) waste from industrial processing, without prejudice to the provisions of article 185, paragraph 1, letter i);
d) waste from artisanal processing;
e) waste from commercial activities;
f) waste from service activities;
g) waste deriving from the activity of recovery and disposal of waste, sludge produced by the potabilization and other treatments of water and by the purification of wastewater and from the abatement of fumes;
h) waste deriving from sanitary activities;
i) deteriorated and obsolete machinery and equipment;
l) end-of-life motor vehicles, trailers and the like and their parts;
m) fuel derived from waste;
n) waste derived from the mechanical selection activities of solid urban waste.
By decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, the list of waste is established, in accordance with art. 1, paragraph 1, letter a), of Directive 75/442/EEC and art. 1, paragraph 4, of Directive 91/689/EC, of which Commission Decision 2000/532/EC of 3 May 2000. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the directive of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea of 9 April 2002, published in the Ordinary Supplement to the Official Gazette no. 108 of 10 May 2002 and reported in Annex D to the fourth part of this decree, continue to apply.
Non-domestic waste expressly indicated as such, with a specific asterisk, in the list of Annex D to the fourth part of this decree, on the basis of Annexes G, H, and I to the same fourth part, is hazardous.
Art. 185
Limits to the scope of application
The following do not fall within the scope of application of the fourth part of this decree:
a) emissions consisting of gaseous effluents emitted into the atmosphere as per article 183, paragraph 1, letter z);
b) water discharges, excluding liquid waste consisting of wastewater;
c) radioactive waste;
d) waste resulting from prospecting, extraction, treatment, storage of mineral resources or from the exploitation of quarries;
e) carcasses and the following agricultural waste: faecal matter and other natural non-hazardous substances used in agricultural activities and in particular lithoid or plant materials and cultivation soil, including in the form of sludge, from the cleaning and washing of plant products reused in normal agricultural practices and for the management of rural lands, even after treatment in farm and inter-farm agricultural plants that reduce the polluting and potentially pathogenic loads of the starting materials;
f) surpluses from the preparation in kitchens of any type of solid, cooked, and raw foods, not entered into the distribution circuit of administration, intended for the shelter facilities for pets as per Law no. 281 of 14 August 1991, in compliance with the current legislation;
g) disused explosive materials;
h) plant materials not contaminated by pollutants from drainage and irrigation ditches, usable as such as a product, in a measure exceeding the limits established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea to be issued within ninety days from the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the limits of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 471 of 25 October 1999 continue to apply;
i) petroleum coke used as fuel for productive use;
l) lithoid material extracted from watercourses, water basins, and riverbeds, following maintenance ordered by the competent authorities;
m) weapon systems, means, materials, and infrastructures directly intended for military defense and national security identified by decree of the Minister of Defense, as well as the management of materials and waste and the remediation of the sites where the cited materials are stored, which remain regulated by the special sector norms in respect of the principles of environmental protection provided for by the fourth part of this decree. The warehouses, deposits, and storage sites where the same materials and waste are kept constitute works intended for military defense not subject to the authorizations and clearances provided for by the fourth part of this decree;
n) materials and infrastructures not included in the ministerial decree of letter m), until the provision of declaration of waste is issued pursuant to the decree of the President of the Republic no. 1076 of 5 June 1976, containing the regulation for the administration and accounting of the organisms of the army, the navy, and the air force.
The discipline of which Regulation (EC) no. 1774/2002 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 3 October 2002, laying down health rules concerning animal by-products not intended for human consumption, which constitutes exhaustive and autonomous discipline in the scope of application indicated therein, remains unaffected.
Art. 186
Excavated earth and rock
Excavated earth and rock, including from tunnels, and the residues from stone processing intended for effective use for backfills, fillings, embankments, and ground materials do not constitute waste and are, therefore, excluded from the scope of application of the fourth part of this decree only in the case where, even when contaminated, during the production cycle, by polluting substances deriving from excavation, drilling, and construction activities, they are used, without preliminary transformations, according to the methods provided for in the project submitted to environmental impact assessment or, if the project is not subject to environmental impact assessment, according to the methods provided for in the project approved by the competent administrative authority, where this is expressly provided, after the opinion of the regional and autonomous province agencies for environmental protection, provided that the average composition of the entire mass does not present a concentration of pollutants higher than the maximum limits provided for by the current norms and by the decree of paragraph 3.
For the purposes of this article, the works whose project is subject to environmental impact assessment constitute a single production cycle, even if the materials of paragraph 1 are intended for different uses, provided that these uses are all provided for in the project.
The respect of the limits of paragraph 1 can be verified, as an alternative to the assessments on the production site, also through assessments on the deposit sites, in case of impossibility of immediate use. The maximum acceptable limits as well as the analysis methods of the materials for their characterization, to be performed according to the criteria of Annex 2 of Title V of the fourth part of this decree, are determined by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea to be issued within ninety days from the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree, unless lower limits are provided for by special provisions. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the acceptable limit concentration values of Annex 1, table 1, column B, of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 471 of 25 October 1999 continue to apply.
The respect of the maximum concentration limits of pollutants of paragraph 3 must be verified through characterization activities of the materials of paragraph 1, to be repeated whenever variations in the production process that originates such materials occur.
For the materials of paragraph 1, for effective use for backfills, fillings, embankments, and ground materials is also intended the destination provided for in the project to different industrial production cycles, as well as the filling of cultivated quarries, or the relocation to another site, for any reason authorized by the competent administrative authority, if this is expressly provided, after, where the relative project is not subject to environmental impact assessment, the opinion of the regional and autonomous province agencies for environmental protection, provided that the limits of paragraph 3 are respected and the relocation is carried out according to project methods of environmental reshaping of the interested territory.
If the materials of paragraph 1 are intended for different industrial production cycles, the administrative authorities competent to exercise the functions of surveillance and control over the same cycles shall verify, without additional charges for public finance, also by carrying out periodic checks, the effective destination for the authorized use of the materials; to this end, the user is required to document their origin, quantity, and specific destination.
For the purposes of the opinion of the regional and autonomous province agencies for environmental protection, of which paragraphs 1 and 5, for projects not subject to environmental impact assessment, a declaration of the subject who carries out the works or of the client, made pursuant to article 47 of the decree of the President of the Republic no. 445 of 28 December 2000, is attached to the request for reuse pursuant to paragraphs 1 to 6, in which it is certified that in the execution of the works no polluting substances have been used, that the reuse occurs without preliminary transformations, that the reuse occurs for one of the works of paragraphs 1 and 5 of this article, as authorized by the competent authority, where this is expressly provided, and that in the excavated material the concentration of pollutants is not higher than the current limits with reference also to the destination site.
In the case where the immediate reuse of the excavated material is not possible, the deposit site of the material, the quantity, the typology of the material must also be indicated, and at the time of reuse, the request must be integrated with what is provided for in paragraphs 6 and 7. The reuse must occur within six months of the deposit, unless an extension is granted upon a motivated request from the interested party.
The opinion of paragraph 5 must be rendered within the peremptory term of thirty days, after which the region shall provide in a substitute capacity upon the request of the interested party.
Waste deriving from the processing of minerals and quarry materials is in no case assimilable to urban waste.

Art. 187
Prohibition of mixing hazardous waste
It is forbidden to mix different categories of hazardous waste of Annex G to the fourth part of this decree or hazardous waste with non-hazardous waste.
By way of derogation from the prohibition of paragraph 1, the mixing of hazardous waste with each other or with other waste, substances, or materials may be authorized pursuant to articles 208, 209, 210, and 211 if the conditions of article 178, paragraph 2, are met, and for the purpose of making the recovery and disposal of waste safer.
Without prejudice to the application of the specific sanctions and in particular those of article 256, paragraph 5, anyone who violates the prohibition of paragraph 1 is required to proceed at his own expense with the separation of the mixed waste if it is technically and economically possible and to satisfy the conditions of article 178, paragraph 2.
Art. 188
Burdens of producers and holders
The burdens relating to the disposal activities are borne by the holder who delivers the waste to an authorized collector or to a subject who carries out the disposal operations, as well as by the previous holders or by the producer of the waste.
The producer or holder of special waste shall fulfill his obligations with the following priorities:
a) self-disposal of the waste;
b) conferment of the waste to third parties authorized pursuant to the current provisions;
c) conferment of the waste to the subjects who manage the public collection service of urban waste, with whom a specific convention has been stipulated;
d) use of rail transport of hazardous waste for distances exceeding three hundred and fifty kilometers and quantities exceeding twenty-five tons;
e) exportation of the waste with the methods provided for in article 194.
The responsibility of the holder for the correct recovery or disposal of the waste is excluded:
a) in case of conferment of the waste to the public collection service;
b) in case of conferment of the waste to subjects authorized for the recovery or disposal activities, provided that the holder has received the form of which article 193 countersigned and dated upon arrival by the recipient within three months from the date of conferment of the waste to the transporter, or at the expiry of the aforesaid term has provided to give communication to the province of the non-receipt of the form. For cross-border shipments of waste, this term is increased to six months and the communication is made to the region.
In the case of conferment of waste to subjects authorized for the operations of grouping, repackaging, and preliminary storage, indicated respectively at points D 13, D 14, D 15 of Annex B to the fourth part of this decree, the responsibility of the producers of the waste for the correct disposal is excluded on condition that the latter, in addition to the transport form of paragraph 3, letter b), have received the certificate of occurred disposal issued by the holder of the plant that carries out the operations of which points from D 1 to D 12 of the cited Annex B. The relative implementation methods are defined by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, which will also have to determine the responsibilities to be attributed to the waste intermediary.
Art. 189
Waste cadastre
The Waste Cadastre, established by art. 3 of decree-law no. 397 of 9 September 1988, converted, with modifications, by law no. 475 of 9 November 1988, is structured into a National Section, based in Rome at the Agency for the Protection of the Environment and for Technical Services (APAT), and into Regional or autonomous province Sections of Trento and Bolzano at the corresponding Regional and autonomous province Agencies for the protection of the environment, and, where such Agencies are not yet established, at the region. The organization norms of the Cadastre are issued and updated by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, within sixty days of the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 372 of 4 August 1998 continue to apply. The implementation of this article shall not result in new or increased charges for public finance.
The Cadastre ensures a complete and constantly updated cognitive framework, also for the purposes of planning waste management activities, of the data collected pursuant to law no. 70 of 25 January 1994, using the nomenclature provided for in the European Catalogue of Waste, of which decision 94/3/EC of 20 December 1993.
Anyone who professionally carries out waste collection and transport activities, including waste traders and intermediaries without detention, or carries out waste recovery and disposal operations, as well as companies and entities that produce hazardous waste and the consortia established for the purpose of recovering particular types of waste, shall communicate annually to the territorially competent Chambers of Commerce, Industry, Handicraft, and Agriculture, with the methods provided for by law no. 70 of 25 January 1994, the quantities and qualitative characteristics of the waste subject to the aforesaid activities. Agricultural entrepreneurs of art. 2135 of the civil code with an annual turnover not exceeding eight thousand euros are exempt from this obligation.
In the case where the producers of hazardous waste confer the same to the public collection service competent for the territory and by special agreement, the communication is made by the service manager limited to the quantity conferred.
The institutional subjects responsible for the integrated urban and assimilated waste management service shall communicate annually, according to the methods provided for by law no. 70 of 25 January 1994, the following information relating to the previous year:
a) the quantity of urban waste collected in their territory;
b) the quantity of special waste collected in their territory following a specific convention with public or private subjects;
c) the subjects who have provided for the management of the waste, specifying the operations carried out, the types and the quantity of waste managed by each;
d) the management and technical and financial amortization costs of the investments for the waste management activities, as well as the proceeds from the tariff of article 238 and the proceeds from the consortia aimed at the recovery of waste;
e) the data relating to separate collection;
f) the quantities collected, divided by materials, in implementation of the agreements with the consortia aimed at the recovery of waste.
The Regional and Provincial Sections and of the autonomous provinces of the Cadastre, on the basis of the data transmitted by the Chambers of Commerce, Industry, Handicraft, and Agriculture, shall provide for the processing of the data and its subsequent transmission to the National Section within thirty days of receipt, pursuant to article 2, paragraph 2, of law no. 70 of 25 January 1994, of the information of paragraphs 3 and 4. The Agency for the Protection of the Environment and for Technical Services (APAT) processes the data, highlighting the types and quantities of waste produced, collected, transported, recovered, and disposed of, as well as the disposal and recovery plants in operation and ensures its publicity.
For the communications relating to packaging waste, the provisions of article 220, paragraph 2, apply.
Art. 190
Loading and unloading registers
The subjects referred to in article 189, paragraph 3, have the obligation to keep a loading and unloading register on which they must record the information on the qualitative and quantitative characteristics of the waste, to be used for the purposes of the annual communication to the Cadastre. The subjects who produce non-hazardous waste of article 184, paragraph 3, letters c), d), and g), have the obligation to keep a loading and unloading register on which they must record the information on the qualitative and quantitative characteristics of the waste. The annotations must be made:
a) for producers, at least within ten working days from the production of the waste and from its unloading;
b) for the subjects who carry out the collection and transport, at least within ten working days from the carrying out of the transport;
c) for traders, intermediaries, and consortia, at least within ten working days from the carrying out of the relative transaction;
d) for the subjects who carry out the recovery and disposal operations, within two working days of taking charge of the waste.
The register kept by the establishments and companies that carry out waste disposal and recovery activities must, moreover, contain:
a) the origin, quantity, characteristics, and specific destination of the waste;
b) the date of loading and unloading of the waste and the means of transport used;
c) the treatment method employed.
The registers are kept at each plant of production, storage, recovery, and disposal of waste, as well as at the headquarters of the companies that carry out collection and transport activities, as well as at the headquarters of the traders and intermediaries. The registers integrated with the forms of article 193 relating to the transport of waste are kept for five years from the date of the last registration, with the exception of the registers relating to the waste disposal operations in landfills, which must be kept indefinitely and at the end of the activity must be delivered to the authority that issued the authorization.
The subjects whose annual production of waste does not exceed ten tons of non-hazardous waste and two tons of hazardous waste may fulfill the obligation of keeping the loading and unloading registers of waste also through the interested category organizations or their service companies that provide to record the data provided with monthly frequency, keeping at the company headquarters a copy of the transmitted data.
The information contained in the register shall be made available at any time to the control authority that requests it.
The registers are numbered, stamped, and managed with the procedures and methods established by the legislation on VAT registers. The obligations connected with the keeping of the loading and unloading registers are considered correctly fulfilled also if A4 format paper, regularly numbered, is used.
The national discipline relating to this article is defined by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea within sixty days from the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 148 of 1 April 1998, as amended by paragraph 9, and of the circular of the Minister of the Environment of 4 August 1998, continue to apply.
The organizations of articles 221, paragraph 3, letters a) and c), 223, 224, 228, 233, 234, 235 and 236, are exempt from the obligation of paragraph 1, provided that they have documentary or accounting evidence with similar functions and without prejudice to the documentary and accounting fulfillments provided for the aforesaid subjects by the current norms.
In Annex 6.C1, section III, letter c), of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 148 of 1 April 1998, after the words: "in liters" the conjunction: "and" is replaced by the disjunction: "or".

Art. 191
Contingent and urgent ordinances and substitute powers
Without prejudice to the provisions in force regarding environmental, health, and public safety protection, with particular reference to the provisions on the power of ordinance of art. 5 of Law no. 225 of 24 February 1992, establishing the national civil protection service, if situations of exceptional and urgent need for the protection of public health and the environment occur, and it is not otherwise possible to provide, the President of the Regional Council or the President of the province or the Mayor may issue, within their respective competencies, contingent and urgent ordinances to allow temporary recourse to special forms of waste management, including in derogation of the provisions in force, ensuring a high level of health and environmental protection. These ordinances are communicated to the President of the Council of Ministers, to the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, to the Minister of Health, to the Minister of Productive Activities, to the President of the region, and to the area authority of article 201 within three days of their issuance and are effective for a period not exceeding six months.
Within one hundred and twenty days of the adoption of the ordinances of paragraph 1, the President of the Regional Council promotes and adopts the necessary initiatives to guarantee separate collection, reuse, recycling, and disposal of waste. In case of futile passage of the term and of ascertained inactivity, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall warn the President of the Regional Council to provide within a suitable term and, in case of prolonged inertia, may adopt in a substitute capacity all the necessary initiatives for the aforesaid purposes.
The ordinances of paragraph 1 indicate the norms to which it is intended to derogate and are adopted on the opinion of the local technical or technical-sanitary bodies, which express themselves with specific reference to the environmental consequences.
The ordinances of paragraph 1 cannot be reiterated for more than two times. If proven needs arise, the President of the region in agreement with the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea may adopt, dictating specific prescriptions, the ordinances of paragraph 1 also beyond the aforesaid terms.
The ordinances of paragraph 1 that allow temporary recourse to special forms of hazardous waste management are communicated by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea to the Commission of the European Union.
Art. 192
Prohibition of abandonment
The abandonment and uncontrolled deposit of waste on the ground and in the ground are prohibited.
It is also forbidden to release waste of any kind, in solid or liquid state, into surface and groundwater.
Without prejudice to the application of the sanctions of articles 255 and 256, anyone who violates the prohibitions of paragraphs 1 and 2 is required to proceed with the removal, the start to recovery or disposal of the waste and the restoration of the state of the places jointly and severally with the owner and with the holders of real or personal rights of enjoyment on the area, to whom this violation is attributable by intent or fault, on the basis of the checks carried out, in an adversarial process with the interested subjects, by the subjects responsible for the control. The Mayor orders with an ordinance the necessary operations for this purpose and the term within which to provide, after which he proceeds with the execution at the expense of the obligated subjects and the recovery of the advanced sums.
If the responsibility for the illicit act is attributable to administrators or representatives of a legal person pursuant to and for the effects of paragraph 3, the legal person and the subjects who have succeeded to the rights of the person himself are jointly and severally liable, according to the provisions of legislative decree no. 231 of 8 June 2001, on the administrative responsibility of legal persons, companies, and associations.
Art. 193
Transport of waste
During transport carried out by entities or companies, waste is accompanied by an identification form from which at least the following data must result:
a) name and address of the producer and holder;
b) origin, type, and quantity of the waste;
c) destination plant;
d) date and route of the shipment;
e) name and address of the recipient.
The identification form of paragraph 1 must be drawn up in four copies, compiled, dated, and signed by the producer or holder of the waste and countersigned by the transporter. A copy of the form must remain with the producer or holder and the other three, countersigned and dated upon arrival by the recipient, are acquired one by the recipient and two by the transporter, who provides to transmit one to the holder. The copies of the form must be kept for five years.
During collection and transport, hazardous waste must be packaged and labeled in accordance with the current norms on the matter.
The provisions of paragraph 1 do not apply to the transport of urban waste carried out by the subject who manages the public service nor to the transport of non-hazardous waste carried out by the producer of the waste itself, occasionally and sporadically, not exceeding the quantity of thirty kilograms or thirty liters.
The national discipline relating to this article is defined by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea to be issued within sixty days of the entry into force of the fourth part of this decree. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 145 of 1 April 1998 continue to apply.
The definition of the model and contents of the identification form and the methods of numbering, stamping, and management of the identification forms, as well as the discipline of the specific responsibilities of the producer or holder, of the transporter, and of the recipient are established by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, taking into account the specific modalities of the individual types of transport, with particular reference to intermodal transport, rail transport, and micro-collection. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the following provisions continue to apply:
a) regarding the definition of the model and contents of the identification form, the decree of the Minister of the Environment no. 145 of 1 April 1998 applies;
b) regarding numbering and stamping, the identification forms must be numbered and stamped by the offices of the Revenue Agency or by the Chambers of Commerce, Industry, Handicraft, and Agriculture or by the competent regional and provincial offices for waste and must be noted on the VAT purchase register. The stamping of the aforesaid identification forms is free and is not subject to any right or tax.
The form of this article is validly replaced, for waste subject to cross-border shipments, by the documents provided for by the community legislation of article 194, including with regard to the route taken on national territory.
The provisions of this article do not apply to the cases regulated by legislative decree no. 99 of 27 January 1992, relating to sludge in agriculture, compatible with the discipline of regulation (EEC) no. 259/1993 of 1 February 1993.
The movement of waste exclusively within private areas is not considered transport for the purposes of the fourth part of this decree.
The commercial document, of art. 7 of regulation (EC) no. 1774/2002 of the European Parliament and of the Council, for operators subject to the obligation of keeping the loading and unloading registers of article 190, replaces for all purposes the identification form of paragraph 1.
The micro-collection of waste, understood as the collection of waste by a single collector or transporter from multiple producers or holders carried out with the same vehicle, must be carried out in the shortest technically possible time. In the identification forms of the waste, all the intermediate stops planned must be indicated in the space relating to the route. In the case where the route should undergo variations, the route actually taken must be indicated in the space relating to the annotations by the transporter.
The stop during the transport of the loaded waste for shipment inside the ports and railway yards, of the departure, sorting, and arrival stations, the stationing of the vehicles in transport configuration, as well as the technical stops for transshipment operations, do not fall within the storage activities of article 183, paragraph 1, letter l), provided that they are dictated by transport needs and do not exceed forty-eight hours, excluding from the calculation the days closed to traffic.
The identification form of waste of paragraph 1 replaces for all purposes the model F of the ministerial decree no. 392 of 16 May 1996.
Art. 194
Transboundary shipments
Transboundary shipments of waste are regulated by the community regulations that regulate the matter, by the bilateral agreements of art. 19 of regulation (EEC) no. 259 of 1 February 1993, and by the decree of paragraph 3.
The agreements in force between the State of the Vatican City, the Republic of San Marino, and the Italian Republic are saved, pursuant to article 19 of the aforesaid regulation (EEC) no. 259 of 1 February 1993. The provisions of art. 20 of the aforesaid regulation do not apply to the imports of solid urban and assimilated waste from the State of the Vatican City and the Republic of San Marino.
By decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Productive Activities, of Health, of Economy and Finance, of Infrastructure and Transport, in compliance with the norms of regulation (EEC) no. 259 of 1 February 1993, the following are regulated:
a) the criteria for calculating the minimum amounts of the financial guarantees to be provided for the shipments of waste, of art. 27 of the aforesaid regulation; these guarantees are reduced by fifty percent for companies registered pursuant to regulation (EC) no. 761/2001, of the European Parliament and of the Council, of 19 March 2001 (Emas), and by forty percent in the case of companies in possession of the environmental certification pursuant to the Uni En Iso 14001 standard;
b) the administrative expenses charged to the notifiers pursuant to art. 33, paragraph 1, of the regulation;
c) the specific modalities for the transport of waste in the States of paragraph 2;
d) the modalities for verifying the application of the principle of proximity for waste destined for disposal.
Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the interministerial decree no. 370 of 3 September 1998 continue to apply.
Pursuant to and for the effects of regulation (EEC) no. 259 of 1 February 1993:
a) the competent authorities of dispatch and destination are the regions and autonomous provinces;
b) the transit authority is the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea;
c) the correspondent is the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea.
The regions and autonomous provinces communicate the information of art. 38 of regulation (EEC) no. 259 of 1 February 1993 to the Ministry of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea for its subsequent forwarding to the Commission of the European Union, as well as, by 30 September of each year, the data, referring to the previous year, provided for by article 13, paragraph 3, of the Basel Convention, ratified by law no. 340 of 18 August 1993.
To the ferrous and non-ferrous scrap of article 183, paragraph 1, letter u), the provisions of article 212, paragraph 12, apply.
CHAPTER II - COMPETENCIES
Art. 195
Competencies of the state
Without prejudice to the further state competencies provided for by special provisions, including those contained in the fourth part of this decree, the following pertain to the State:
a) the functions of guidance and coordination necessary for the implementation of the fourth part of this decree, to be exercised pursuant to art. 8 of law no. 59 of 15 March 1997, within the limits of what is established by article 8, paragraph 6, of law no. 131 of 5 June 2003;
b) the definition of the general criteria and methodologies for the integrated management of waste, as well as the identification of the needs for the disposal of sanitary waste, also for the purpose of reducing its movement;
c) the identification of the initiatives and measures to prevent and limit, including through recourse to forms of security deposit on goods placed on the market, the production of waste, as well as to reduce its hazardousness;
d) the identification of the homogeneous flows of waste production with a higher environmental impact, which present the greatest difficulties of disposal or particular possibilities of recovery both for the substances used in the base products and for the overall quantity of the waste itself;
e) the adoption of general criteria for the drafting of sector plans for the reduction, recycling, recovery, and optimization of waste flows;
f) the identification, in respect of the constitutional attributions of the regions, of the recovery and disposal plants of pre-eminent national interest to be realized for the modernization and development of the country; the identification is carried out, after consulting the Unified Conference of article 8 of legislative decree no. 281 of 28 August 1997, by means of a program, adopted by decree of the President of the Council of Ministers on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, and inserted in the Economic and Financial Programming Document, with an indication of the necessary allocations for their realization. In identifying the strategic infrastructures and settlements of this paragraph, the Government proceeds according to the purposes of socio-economic rebalancing between the areas of the national territory. The Government indicates in the draft financial law pursuant to article 11, paragraph 3, letter i-ter), of law no. 468 of 5 August 1978, the necessary resources, also for the purpose of disbursing the compensatory contributions in favor of the local authorities, which integrate the public, community, and private financing available for this purpose;
g) the definition, in respect of the constitutional attributions of the regions, of a national plan of communication and environmental knowledge. The definition is carried out, after consulting the Unified Conference of article 8 of legislative decree no. 281 of 28 August 1997, by means of a Program, formulated by decree of the President of the Council of Ministers, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, inserted in the Economic and Financial Programming Document, with an indication of the necessary allocations for the realization;
h) the indication of the types of measures aimed at encouraging the rationalization of the collection, sorting, and recycling of waste;
i) the identification of initiatives and actions, including economic ones, to favor the recycling and recovery of secondary raw material from waste, as well as to promote the market for materials recovered from waste and their use by public administrations and economic subjects, including pursuant to art. 52, paragraph 56, letter a), of law no. 448 of 28 December 2001, and of the decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea no. 203 of 8 May 2003;
l) the identification of quality objectives of waste management services;
m) the determination of general criteria, differentiated for urban waste and for special waste, for the purpose of the elaboration of the regional plans of article 199 with particular reference to the determination, in agreement with the State-regions Conference, of the guidelines for the identification of the Optimal territorial areas, to be constituted pursuant to article 200, and for the coordination of the plans themselves;
n) the determination, regarding the assignment of the concession of the service for the integrated management of waste, in agreement with the State-regions Conference, of the guidelines for the definition of the tenders, and in particular of the admission requirements of the companies, and of the relative specifications, including with reference to the economic elements relating to the existing plants;
o) the determination, in agreement with the State-regions Conference, of the guidelines concerning the forms and modes of cooperation between the local authorities, including with reference to the collection of the tariff on urban waste falling within the same optimal territorial area, according to criteria of transparency, efficiency, effectiveness, and economy;
p) the indication of the general criteria relating to the characteristics of the areas not suitable for the location of waste disposal plants;
q) the indication of the general criteria for the organization and implementation of the separate collection of urban waste;
r) the determination, in agreement with the State-regions Conference, of the guidelines, the general criteria, and the standards for the remediation of contaminated sites, as well as the determination of the criteria to identify the remediation interventions which, in relation to the significance of the environmental impact connected with the extension of the interested area, to the quantity and hazardousness of the pollutants present, are of national interest;
s) the determination of the calculation methodologies and the definition of recycled material for the implementation of article 196, paragraph 1, letter p);
t) the adaptation of the fourth part of this decree to the directives, decisions, and regulations of the European Union.
The following are also of state competence:
a) the indication of the criteria and modalities of adoption, according to principles of unity, completeness, and coordination, of the technical norms for the management of waste, of hazardous waste, and of specific types of waste, with reference also to the relative accreditation and certification systems pursuant to article 178, paragraph 5;
b) the adoption of the norms and conditions for the application of the simplified procedures of articles 214, 215, and 216, including the guidelines containing the specification of the report to be attached to the communication provided for by those articles;
c) the determination of the limits of acceptability and of the chemical, physical, and biological characteristics of certain substances contained in the waste in relation to specific uses of the same;
d) the determination and the discipline of the recovery activities of asbestos products and of the goods and products containing asbestos, by decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Health and with the Minister of Productive Activities;
e) the determination of the qualitative and quantitative criteria for the assimilation, for the purposes of collection and disposal, of special waste to urban waste, deriving from entities and companies operating on areas with a surface area not exceeding 150 square meters in municipalities with a resident population of less than 10,000 inhabitants, or a surface area not exceeding 250 square meters in municipalities with a resident population of more than 10,000 inhabitants. The waste that is formed in the production areas, including the warehouses of raw materials and finished products, cannot normally be assimilated to urban waste, except for the waste produced in the offices, in the canteens, in the company stores, in the bars, and in the premises at the service of the workers or in any case open to the public;
f) the adoption of a uniform model of the certificate of occurred disposal issued by the plant owner which will have to indicate for each load and/or conferment the disposed quota in relation to the authorized annual capacity of the same plant;
g) the definition of the methods, procedures, and standards for the sampling and analysis of waste;
h) the determination of the technical and financial requirements and capacities for the exercise of waste management activities, including the general criteria for the determination of the financial guarantees in favor of the regions, with particular reference to those of the subjects subject to registration with the Register of article 212, according to the modality of paragraph 9 of the same article;
i) the reorganization and keeping of the National Waste Cadastre;
l) the definition of the model and contents of the form of article 193 and the regulation of waste transport, including the identification of the types of waste that for proven technical, environmental, and economic reasons must be transported by rail;
m) the identification of the types of waste that for proven technical, environmental, and economic reasons can be disposed of directly in landfills;
n) the adoption of a uniform model of the register of article 190 and the definition of the modalities for keeping it, as well as the identification of any documents substituting for the register itself;
o) the identification of electrical and electronic waste, of article 227, paragraph 1, letter a);
p) the updating of the Annexes to the fourth part of this decree;
q) the adoption of the technical norms, the modalities, and the conditions of use of the product obtained through composting, with particular reference to the agronomic use as fertilizer, pursuant to law no. 748 of 19 October 1984, and of the quality product obtained through composting from organic waste selected at the source with separate collection;
r) the authorization for the disposal of waste in marine waters, in accordance with the provisions established by the community norms and the international conventions in force on the matter, issued by the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea on the proposal of the maritime authority in whose area of competence the port closest to the place where the disposal is to be carried out is located or the port from which the ship with the load of waste to be disposed of departs;
s) the identification of the measure of the absorbent and neutralizing substances, previously tested by Universities or specialized Institutes, with which the plants intended for the storage, recharging, maintenance, deposit, and replacement of accumulators must be equipped in order to prevent the pollution of the soil, of the subsoil and to avoid damage to health and the environment deriving from the leakage of acid, taking into account the size of the plants, the number of accumulators and the risk of spillage connected with the type of activity carried out.
3. Unless otherwise provided by the fourth part of this decree, the functions of paragraph 1 are exercised pursuant to law no. 400 of 23 August 1988, on the proposal of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Productive Activities, of Health, and of the Interior, having heard the State-regions Conference, the regions, and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano.
4. Unless otherwise provided by the fourth part of this decree, the regulatory and technical norms of paragraph 2 are adopted, pursuant to art. 17, paragraph 3, of law no. 400 of 23 August 1988, with decrees of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Productive Activities, of Health, and of the Interior, as well as, when the aforesaid norms concern agricultural waste and the transport of waste, in concert, respectively, with the Ministers of Agricultural and Forestry Policies and of Infrastructure and Transport.
5. Without prejudice to what is provided by legislative decree no. 112 of 31 March 1998, for the purposes of surveillance and ascertainment of the illicit acts in violation of the legislation on waste as well as the repression of illicit trafficking and illegal disposal of waste, the Carabinieri Command for the protection of the environment (C.C.T.A.) and the Corps of the Port Captaincies shall act; the State Forestry Corps may also intervene, and the Guardia di Finanza and the State Police may contribute.

**Art. 196**
**Competencies of the regions**
1. The following are of the competence of the regions, in respect of the principles provided for by the current legislation and by the fourth part of this decree, including those of article 195:
a) the preparation, adoption, and updating, having heard the provinces, the municipalities, and the Area Authorities, of the regional waste management plans, of article 199;
b) the regulation of waste management activities, including the separate collection of urban waste, including hazardous waste, according to a general criterion of separation of waste of food origin and of scraps of plant and animal products or in any case with a high moisture content from the remaining waste;
c) the elaboration, approval, and updating of the plans for the remediation of contaminated areas of their competence;
d) the approval of the projects of new plants for the management of waste, including hazardous waste, and the authorization for the modifications of existing plants, without prejudice to the state competencies of article 195, paragraph 1, letter f);
e) the authorization for the exercise of the disposal and recovery operations of waste, including hazardous waste;
f) the activities in the matter of transboundary shipments of waste that regulation (EEC) no. 259/93 of 1 February 1993 attributes to the competent authorities of dispatch and destination;
g) the delimitation, in respect of the general guidelines of article 195, paragraph 1, letter m), of the optimal territorial areas for the management of urban and assimilated waste;
h) the drafting of guidelines and criteria for the preparation and approval of the remediation and safety projects, as well as the identification of the types of projects not subject to authorization, in respect of what is provided for in article 195, paragraph 1, letter r);
i) the promotion of the integrated management of waste;
l) the incentive for the reduction of waste production and for its recovery;
m) the specification of the contents of the report to be attached to the communication of articles 214, 215, and 216, in respect of guidelines elaborated pursuant to article 195, paragraph 2, letter b);
n) the definition of criteria for the identification, by the provinces, of the areas not suitable for the location of waste disposal and recovery plants, in respect of the general criteria indicated in article 195, paragraph 1, letter p);
o) the definition of the criteria for the identification of the places or plants suitable for disposal and the determination, in respect of the technical norms of article 195, paragraph 2, letter a), of special provisions for waste of a particular type;
p) the adoption, on the basis of a calculation methodology and criteria established by a specific decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Ministers of Productive Activities and of Health, having heard the Minister for Regional Affairs, to be issued within sixty days from the date of entry into force of the fourth part of this decree, of the provisions necessary so that the public entities and the companies with a prevalent public capital, including those managing services, cover their annual need for manufactured goods and goods, indicated in the same decree, with a quota of products obtained from recycled material not less than 30 percent of the same need. To this end, the aforesaid subjects shall insert in the tender notices or in the selection notices for the award of specific preference clauses, on equal terms with the other requirements and conditions. Until the issuance of the aforesaid decree, the provisions of the decree of the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea no. 203 of 8 May 2003, and subsequent implementation circulars, continue to apply. In the meantime, the existing regional provisions remain in force.
2. For the exercise of the functions of paragraph 1, the regions shall also avail themselves of the regional agencies for environmental protection.
3. The regions shall favor the realization of waste disposal and recovery plants in industrial areas, compatible with the characteristics of the areas themselves, encouraging self-disposal initiatives. This provision does not apply to landfills.

**Art. 197**
**Competencies of the provinces**
1. In implementation of art. 19 of legislative decree no. 267 of 18 August 2000, the provinces are competent for:
a) the control and verification of the remediation interventions and the monitoring consequent to them;
b) the periodic control over all waste management, intermediation, and trade activities, including the ascertainment of the violations of the provisions of the fourth part of this decree;
c) the verification and control of the requirements provided for the application of the simplified procedures, with the modalities of articles 214, 215, and 216;
d) the identification, on the basis of the provisions of the territorial coordination plan of article 20, paragraph 2, of legislative decree no. 267 of 18 August 2000, if already adopted, and of the provisions of article 199, paragraph 3, letters d) and h), as well as having heard the Area Authority and the municipalities, of the zones suitable for the location of waste disposal plants, as well as of the zones not suitable for the location of waste recovery and disposal plants.
2. For the exercise of their functions, the provinces may avail themselves, by means of specific conventions, of public bodies, including the Regional Agencies for Environmental Protection (ARPA), with specific experience and technical skills on the matter, without prejudice to what is provided for in articles 214, 215, and 216 in the matter of simplified procedures.
3. The control officers are authorized to carry out inspections, verifications, and sample collections within establishments, plants, or companies that produce or that carry out waste management activities. The industrial secret cannot be opposed to the control officers, who are, in turn, held to the obligation of confidentiality pursuant to the current legislation.
4. The personnel belonging to the Carabinieri Command for the protection of the environment (C.C.T.A.) is authorized to carry out the necessary inspections and verifications for the purpose of the performance of the functions of art. 8 of law no. 349 of 8 July 1986, establishing the Ministry of the Environment.
5. Within the competencies of paragraph 1, the provinces shall subject to adequate periodic controls the establishments and companies that dispose of or recover waste, ensuring, in particular, that adequate periodic controls are carried out on the activities subject to the simplified procedures of articles 214, 215, and 216 and that the controls concerning the collection and transport of hazardous waste concern, in the first place, the origin and destination of the waste.
6. The other provisions in force on surveillance and control provided for by special provisions remain unaffected.

**Art. 198**
**Competencies of the municipalities**
1. The municipalities contribute, within the activities carried out at the level of the optimal territorial areas of article 200 and with the modalities provided therein, to the management of urban and assimilated waste. Until the start of the activities of the subject awarded the public tender called by the Area Authority pursuant to article 202, the municipalities shall continue the management of urban waste and of assimilated waste sent for disposal under a monopoly regime in the forms of article 113, paragraph 5, of legislative decree no. 267 of 18 August 2000.
2. The municipalities contribute to regulating the management of urban waste with specific regulations which, in respect of the principles of transparency, efficiency, effectiveness, and economy and in coherence with the area plans adopted pursuant to article 201, paragraph 3, establish in particular:
a) the measures to ensure hygienic-sanitary protection in all phases of the management of urban waste;
b) the modalities of the collection and transport service of urban waste;
c) the modalities of the conferment, of the separate collection and of the transport of urban and assimilated waste in order to guarantee a distinct management of the different fractions of waste and to promote their recovery;
d) the norms aimed at guaranteeing a distinct and adequate management of hazardous urban waste and of waste from exhumation and disinterment of article 184, paragraph 2, letter f);
e) the necessary measures to optimize the forms of conferment, collection, and transport of primary packaging waste in synergy with other commodity fractions, setting minimum standards to be respected;
f) the modalities of execution of the weighing of urban waste before sending it for recovery and disposal;
g) the assimilation, for quality and quantity, of special non-hazardous waste to urban waste, according to the criteria of article 195, paragraph 2, letter e), without prejudice to the definitions of article 184, paragraph 2, letters c) and d).
3. The municipalities are required to provide the region, the province, and the Area Authorities with all the information on the management of urban waste requested by them.
4. The municipalities are also required to express their opinion regarding the approval of the remediation projects of contaminated sites issued by the regions.

**CHAPTER III - INTEGRATED WASTE MANAGEMENT SERVICE**

**Art. 199**
**Regional plans**
1. The regions, having heard the provinces, the municipalities, and, with regard to urban waste, the Area Authorities of article 201, in respect of the principles and purposes of articles 177, 178, 179, 180, 181, and 182 and in conformity with the general criteria established by article 195, paragraph 1, letter m) and with those provided for in this article, shall prepare regional waste management plans ensuring adequate publicity and the maximum participation of citizens, pursuant to law no. 241 of 7 August 1990.
2. The regional waste management plans provide for measures aimed at reducing the quantities, volumes, and hazardousness of waste.
3. The regional waste management plans also provide for:
a) the conditions and technical criteria on the basis of which, in respect of the provisions in force on the matter, the plants for the management of waste, with the exception of landfills, can be located in the areas intended for productive settlements;
b) the typology and the complex of the disposal and recovery plants for urban waste to be realized in the region, taking into account the objective of ensuring the management of non-hazardous urban waste within the optimal territorial areas of article 200, as well as the offer of disposal and recovery from the industrial system;
c) the delimitation of each single optimal territorial area on the regional territory, in respect of the guidelines of article 195, paragraph 1, letter m);
d) the complex of the activities and the needs of the necessary plants to guarantee the management of urban waste according to criteria of transparency, efficiency, effectiveness, economy, and self-sufficiency of the management of non-hazardous urban waste within each of the optimal territorial areas of article 200, as well as to ensure the disposal of special waste in places close to those of production in order to favor the reduction of the movement of waste;
e) the promotion of the management of waste for optimal territorial areas through an adequate discipline of incentives, providing for the most deserving areas, taking into account the available resources under current legislation, a maggioration of contributions; to this end, the regions may establish a special fund in their budgets;
f) the prescriptions against soil pollution and the deposit on the ground of landfills of civil and industrial waste that may in any case affect the quality of surface and groundwater bodies, in respect of the prescriptions dictated pursuant to article 65, paragraph 3, letter f);
g) the estimate of the costs of the urban waste recovery and disposal operations;
h) the criteria for the identification, by the provinces, of the areas not suitable for the location of waste recovery and disposal plants as well as for the identification of the places or plants suitable for the disposal of waste, in respect of the general criteria of article 195, paragraph 1, letter p);
i) the initiatives aimed at limiting the production of waste and at favoring the reuse, recycling, and recovery of waste;
l) the initiatives aimed at favoring the recovery from waste of materials and energy;
m) the measures aimed at promoting the regionalization of the collection, sorting, and disposal of urban waste;
n) the types, quantities, and origin of the waste to be recovered or disposed of, divided by single optimal territorial area with regard to urban waste;
o) the determination, in respect of the technical norms of article 195, paragraph 2, letter a), of special provisions for waste of a particular type, including those of article 225, paragraph 6;
p) the general technical requirements relating to waste management activities in respect of the national and community legislation.
4. The regional waste management plan is coordinated with the other planning instruments of regional competence provided for by the current legislation, where adopted.
5. The plans for the remediation of contaminated areas, which must provide for, are an integral part of the regional plan:
a) the order of priority of the interventions, based on a risk assessment criterion elaborated by the Agency for the Protection of the Environment and for Technical Services (APAT);
b) the identification of the sites to be remediated and the general characteristics of the pollutants present;
c) the modalities of the remediation and environmental restoration interventions, which give priority to the use of materials from urban waste recovery activities;
d) the estimate of the financial burdens;
e) the modalities of disposal of the materials to be removed.
6. The approval of the regional plan or its adaptation is a necessary requirement to access national funding.
7. The region approves or adapts the plan within two years from the date of entry into force of the fourth part of this decree; in the meantime, the current regional plans remain in force.
8. In case of futile passage of the term of paragraph 7 and of ascertained inactivity, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall warn the competent regional bodies to comply within a suitable term and, in case of prolonged inertia, shall adopt, in a substitute capacity, the necessary provisions for the elaboration and approval of the regional plan.
9. If the competent authorities do not realize the interventions provided for by the regional plan in the terms and with the modalities established and such omissions may cause serious prejudice to the implementation of the plan itself, the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea shall warn the defaulting authorities to provide within a term of not less than one hundred and eighty days. After said term has passed without effect, the Minister may adopt, in a substitute capacity, all the necessary and suitable provisions for the implementation of the interventions contained in the plan. To this end, he may also avail himself of "ad acta" commissioners.
10. The provisions of paragraph 9 may concern interventions aimed at:
a) implementing the separate collection of waste;
b) providing for the re-employment, recovery, and recycling of packaging conferred to the public service;
c) favoring urban waste treatment operations for the purpose of recycling and recovering the same;
d) favoring the realization and use of plants for the recovery of solid urban waste.
11. The regions, having heard the interested provinces, in agreement with each other or individually, for the purposes of the fourth part of this decree shall provide for the updating of the plan as well as for the programming of the necessary implementing interventions in accordance with the procedures and within the limits of the resources provided for by the current legislation.
12. On the basis of specific program agreements stipulated with the Minister of the Environment and for the Protection of the Land and Sea, in concert with the Minister of Productive Activities, in agreement with the interested region, the construction and operation, or only the operation, within existing industrial settlements, of plants for the recovery of urban waste not provided for by the regional plan may be authorized, pursuant to articles 214 and 216, if the following conditions are met:
a) waste from separate collection is recycled and recovered as a primary raw material, or compost is produced from waste or fuel is used from waste;
b) the technical norms of articles 214 and 216 are respected;
c) the best technologies for environmental protection are used;
d) a reduction of polluting emissions is guaranteed.

**Art. 200**
**Territorial organization of the integrated urban waste management service**
1. The management of urban waste is organized on the basis of optimal territorial areas, hereinafter also referred to as ATO, delimited by the regional plan of article 199, in respect of the guidelines of article 195, paragraph 1, letters m), n), and o), and according to the following criteria:
a) overcoming the fragmentation of managements through an integrated waste management service;
b) achieving adequate management dimensions, defined on the basis of physical, demographic, technical parameters and on the basis of political-administrative divisions;
c) adequate evaluation of the road and railway communication system in order to optimize transport within the ATO;
d) valorization of common needs and affinities in the production and management of waste;
e) recognition of already realized and functioning waste management plants;
f) consideration of the previous delimitations so that the new ATOs deviate from the previous ones only on the basis of motivated needs of efficiency, effectiveness, and economy.
2. The regions, having heard the interested provinces and municipalities, within the framework of the programming and planning activities of their competence, within the term of six months from the date of entry into force of the fourth part of this decree, shall provide for the delimitation of the optimal territorial areas, in respect of the guidelines of article 195, paragraph 1, letter m). The provision is communicated to the interested provinces and municipalities.
3. The interested regions, in agreement with each other, shall delimit the ATOs if they are included in the territory of two or more regions.
4. The regions shall regulate the control, including in a substitute capacity, of the waste management operations, of the functionality of the relative plants, and of the respect of the limits and prescriptions provided for by the relative authorizations.
5. The cities or agglomerations of municipalities, of dimensions greater than the average ones of a single area, can be subdivided taking into account the criteria of paragraph 1.
6. The single municipalities within thirty days from the communication of paragraph 2 can submit motivated and documented requests for modification to the assignment to a specific territorial area and for a shift to a different territorial area, bordering on that of assignment.
7. The regions may adopt alternative models or in derogation of the model of the Optimal Territorial Areas where they prepare a regional waste plan that demonstrates its adequacy with respect to the strategic objectives provided for by the current legislation, with particular reference to the general criteria and the guidelines reserved, on the matter, to the State pursuant to article 195.

**Art. 201**
**Discipline of the integrated urban waste management service**
1. For the purpose of organizing the integrated urban waste management service, the regions and the autonomous provinces of Trento and Bolzano, within the term of six months from the date of entry into force of the fourth part of this decree, shall regulate the forms and modes of cooperation between the local authorities falling within the same optimal area, providing that they themselves constitute the Area Authorities of paragraph 2, to which the organization, the entrustment, and the control of the integrated waste management service are delegated, in respect of the principle of coordination with the competencies of the other public administrations.
2. The Area Authority is a structure with legal personality constituted in each optimal territorial area delimited by the competent region, to which the local authorities mandatorily participate and to which the exercise of their competencies in the matter of integrated waste management is transferred.
3. The Area Authority organizes the service and determines the objectives to be pursued to guarantee its management according to criteria of efficiency, effectiveness, economy, and transparency; to this end, it adopts a specific area plan in accordance with what is provided for in article 203, paragraph 3.
